"     1\u2192/*\n     2\u2192 * EduPay Ledger Academy\n     3\u2192 * Shared Kernel / Domain / Money\n     4\u2192 *\n     5\u2192 * Copyright (c) 2023-2024 EduPay\n     6\u2192 *\n     7\u2192 * This file defines the canonical Money value-object used across every\n     8\u2192 * bounded-context (Admissions, Bursar, Financial-Aid, etc.).  The structure is\n     9\u2192 * purposely framework-agnostic so that educators can swap persistence layers,\n    10\u2192 * message brokers, or UI shells without impacting business rules.\n    11\u2192 *\n    12\u2192 * Design notes\n    13\u2192 * ------------\n    14\u2192 * 1. All operations guarantee currency homogeneity; cross-currency math must\n    19\u2192 *    be handled by the FX service in the multi-currency bounded context.\n    20\u2192 * 4. All side-effects are routed through\n   104\u2192 *  a set of callbacks supplied by the calling application/service.  Each\n   105\u2192 *  callback must be idempotent because the saga might retry crashed steps.\n   106\u2192 *\n   107\u2192 *  Every callback returns `true` on success.  On failure it returns `false`\n   108\u2192 *  and must populate `err_out`.\n   109\u2192 */\n   110\u2192\n   111\u2192typedef bool (*validate_eligibility_fn)(\n   112\u2192        const */\n   158\u2192#define _CHECK_CB(cb) do {                                                  \\\n   159\u2192    if ((cb) == NULL) {                                                     \\\n   160\u2192                                                  \\\n   165\u2192        return false;                                                       \\\n   166\u2192    } } while (0)\n   167\u2192\n   168\u2192/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n   169\u2192/*  Saga Public API                                                           */\n   170\u2192/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n   171\u2192static inline\n   172\u2192bool disburse_stipend_run(\n   173\u2192        const stipend_disbursement_request_t   *req,\n   174\u2192        const stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t *cb,\n   175\u2192        saga_error_t                           *err_out);\n   176\u2192\n   177\u2192/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n   178\u2192/*  Implementation                                                            */\n   179\u2192/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n   180\u2192static inline\n   181\u2192bool disburse_stipend_run(\n   182\u2192        const stipend_disbursement_request_t   *req,\n   183\u2192        const stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t *cb,\n   184\u2192        saga_error_t                           *err_out)\n   185\u2192{\n   186\u2192    /* Defensive programming: never trust caller. */\n   187\u2192    if (!req || !cb) {\n   188\u2192        if (err_out) {\n   189\u2192            err_out->code = SAGA_ERR_INTERNAL;\n   190\u2192            snprintf(err_out->message, sizeof(err_out->message),\n   191\u2192                     \"NULL argument(s) received\");\n   192\u2192        }\n   193\u2192        return false;\n Publish domain event (CQRS / Integration-Event)                 */\n   263\u2192    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n   264\u2192    _CHECK_CB(cb->publish_domain_event);\n   265\u2192    if (!cb->publish_domain_event(req, \"StipendDisbursed\", err_out)) {\n   266\u2192\n   267\u2192        /* Compensation Path #3: ledger reversal + reverse transfer + release budget */\n   268\u2192        _CHECK_CB(cb->record_ledger_entry);\n   269\u2192        _CHECK_CB(cb->reverse_transfer);\n   270\u2192        _CHECK_CB(cb->release_budget);\n   271\u2192\n   272\u2192        saga_error_t cmp_err = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n   273\u2192        cb->record_ledger_entry(req, \"STIPEND_DISBURSEMENT_REVERSED\", network_tx_id, &cmp_err);\n   274\u2192        cb->reverse_transfer(network_tx_id, &cmp_err);\n   275\u2192        cb->release_budget(reservation_id, &cmp_err);\n   276\u2192\n   277\u2192        return false;\n   278\u2192    }\n   279\u2192\n   280\u2192    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n   281\u2192    /* 6. Success!                                                        */\n   282\u2192    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n   283\u2192    if (err_out) {\n   284\u2192        *err_out = SAGA_ERROR_INIT(); /* reset to success */\n   285\u2192    }\n   286\u2192    return true;\n   287\u2192}\n   288\u2192\n   289\u2192/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n   290\u2192/*  Example: Default No-Op Callbacks for Unit-Testing                         */\n   291\u2192/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n   292\u2192#ifdef EDUPAY_STIPEND_SAGA_ENABLE_NOOP_CALLBACKS\n   293\u2192\n   294\u2192#include <string.h>\n   295\u2192\n   296\u2192/* These compile-time helpers allow professors to run the saga in a REPL\n   297\u2192 * without wiring external systems. The code sits in the\n *   Use-Case layer (Clean Architecture) and has zero dependencies on any\n *   concrete frameworks, I/O, or persistence technology. \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n *   \u2502  FinancialAid::DisburseStipendSaga                       \u2502\n *   \u2502-----------------------------------------------------------\u2502\n *   \u2502 validate_eligibility()   \u2500\u2510                               \u2502\n *   \u2502 reserve_budget()          \u251c\u2500\u25ba initiate_transfer() \u2500\u2510      \u2502\n *   \u2502 record_ledger()           \u2502                         \u2502      \u2502\n *   \u2502 publish_event()           \u2502                         \u2502      \u2502\n *   \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518                         \u2502      \u2502\n *                                \u2502                        \u2502      \u2502\n *                                \u25bc                        \u2502      \u2502\n *                         compensation() \u25c4\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518      \u2502\n *     (release_budget, reverse_transfer, ledger_reversal)        \u2502\n *   \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n *\n *   NOTE:\n *     1.  Header-only so that professors can #include it in toy\n *         command-line drivers or embed it in micro-services without\n *         tweaking build systems.\n *     2.  Thread-safe: no global / static mutable state.\n *     3.  Compatible with C89+ (but uses stdint.h & stdbool.h).\n */\n\n#ifndef EDUPAY_LEDGER_ACADEMY_FINANCIAL_AID_DISBURSE_STIPEND_SAGA_H\n#define EDUPAY_LEDGER_ACADEMY_FINANCIAL_AID_DISBURSE_STIPEND_SAGA_H\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Standard Library Includes                                                 */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Domain Types                                                              */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/*\n * ISO-4217 three-letter currency code.  Stored as a fixed-width char[4]\n * where index 3 must be '\\0'.\n */\ntypedef char iso_currency_code_t[4];\n\n/* Forward-declaration for opaque correlation identifiers (UUID, ULID, etc.). */\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t bytes[16];\n} correlation_id_t;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Request DTO                                                               */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\ntypedef struct {\n    uint64_t         student_id;\n    uint64_t         stipend_cents;\n    iso_currency_code_t currency;\n    char             term[8];         /* e.g., \"2024SP\" */\n    correlation_id_t correlation_id;\n    time_t           requested_at_utc;\n} stipend_disbursement_request_t;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Error Handling                                                            */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\ntypedef enum {\n    SAGA_OK = 0,\n    SAGA_ERR_VALIDATION     =  1,\n    SAGA_ERR_INSUFFICIENT   =  2,\n    SAGA_ERR_TRANSFER_FAIL  =  3,\n    SAGA_ERR_LEDGER_FAIL    =  4,\n    SAGA_ERR_EVENT_BUS      =  5,\n    SAGA_ERR_COMPENSATION   =  6,\n    SAGA_ERR_INTERNAL       = 99\n} saga_error_code_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    saga_error_code_t code;\n    char              message[128]; /* ASCII diagnostics. */\n} saga_error_t;\n\n/* Convenience macro for initializing an empty saga_error_t */\n#define SAGA_ERROR_INIT() (saga_error_t){ .code = SAGA_OK, .message = \"\" }\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Saga Orchestration \u2013 Callback VTable                                      */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*\n *  The saga never performs I/O directly.  All side-effects are routed through\n *  a set of callbacks supplied by the calling application/service.  Each\n *  callback must be idempotent because the saga might retry crashed steps.\n *\n *  Every callback returns `true` on success.  On failure it returns `false`\n *  and must populate `err_out`.\n */\n\ntypedef bool (*validate_eligibility_fn)(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n        saga_error_t                         *err_out);\n\ntypedef bool (*reserve_budget_fn)(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n        uint64_t                             *reservation_id_out,\n        saga_error_t                         *err_out);\n\ntypedef bool (*release_budget_fn)(\n        uint64_t       reservation_id,\n        saga_error_t  *err_out);\n\ntypedef bool (*initiate_transfer_fn)(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n        uint64_t                             *network_tx_id_out,\n        saga_error_t                         *err_out);\n\ntypedef bool (*reverse_transfer_fn)(\n        uint64_t       network_tx_id,\n        saga_error_t  *err_out);\n\ntypedef bool (*record_ledger_entry_fn)(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n        const char                           *entry_type,\n        uint64_t                              related_id, /* reservation or tx id */\n        saga_error_t                         *err_out);\n\ntypedef bool (*publish_domain_event_fn)(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n        const char                           *event_name,\n        saga_error_t                         *err_out);\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  VTable Container                                                          */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\ntypedef struct {\n    validate_eligibility_fn   validate_eligibility;\n    reserve_budget_fn         reserve_budget;\n    release_budget_fn         release_budget;\n    initiate_transfer_fn      initiate_transfer;\n    reverse_transfer_fn       reverse_transfer;\n    record_ledger_entry_fn    record_ledger_entry;\n    publish_domain_event_fn   publish_domain_event;\n} stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t;\n\n/* Utility macro to check if a pointer in the vtable is missing at runtime. */\n#define _CHECK_CB(cb) do {                                                  \\\n    if ((cb) == NULL) {                                                     \\\n        if (err_out) {                                                      \\\n            err_out->code = SAGA_ERR_INTERNAL;                              \\\n            snprintf(err_out->message, sizeof(err_out->message),            \\\n                     \"Callback missing: %s\", #cb);                          \\\n        }                                                                   \\\n        return false;                                                       \\\n    } } while (0)\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Saga Public API                                                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline\nbool disburse_stipend_run(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t   *req,\n        const stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t *cb,\n        saga_error_t                           *err_out);\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Implementation                                                            */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline\nbool disburse_stipend_run(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t   *req,\n        const stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t *cb,\n        saga_error_t                           *err_out)\n{\n    /* Defensive programming: never trust caller. */\n    if (!req || !cb) {\n        if (err_out) {\n            err_out->code = SAGA_ERR_INTERNAL;\n            snprintf(err_out->message, sizeof(err_out->message),\n                     \"NULL argument(s) received\");\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    uint64_t reservation_id = 0;\n    uint64_t network_tx_id  = 0;\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 1. Validate eligibility                                            */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->validate_eligibility);\n    if (!cb->validate_eligibility(req, err_out)) {\n        return false; /* validation errors are final, no compensation needed */\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 2. Reserve budget (Financial-Aid allocation ledger)                */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->reserve_budget);\n    if (!cb->reserve_budget(req, &reservation_id, err_out)) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 3. Initiate transfer via payment network                           */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->initiate_transfer);\n    if (!cb->initiate_transfer(req, &network_tx_id, err_out)) {\n\n        /* ------------------------------------------------------------------\n         * Compensation Path #1: release the budget reservation\n         * ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->release_budget);\n        saga_error_t cmp_err = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n        if (!cb->release_budget(reservation_id, &cmp_err)) {\n            /* Fatal: both forward step + compensation failed */\n            if (err_out && err_out->code == SAGA_OK) {\n                *err_out = cmp_err;\n            }\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        return false; /* original error already populated by initiate_transfer */\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 4. Record ledger entry (financial book-keeping)                    */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->record_ledger_entry);\n    if (!cb->record_ledger_entry(req, \"STIPEND_DISBURSEMENT\", network_tx_id, err_out)) {\n\n        /* Compensation Path #2: reverse transfer + release budget */\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->reverse_transfer);\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->release_budget);\n\n        saga_error_t cmp_err1 = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n        if (!cb->reverse_transfer(network_tx_id, &cmp_err1)) {\n            if (err_out && err_out->code == SAGA_OK) *err_out = cmp_err1;\n            /* Deliberately fall through to attempt second compensation */\n        }\n\n        saga_error_t cmp_err2 = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n        if (!cb->release_budget(reservation_id, &cmp_err2)) {\n            if (err_out && err_out->code == SAGA_OK) *err_out = cmp_err2;\n        }\n\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 5. Publish domain event (CQRS / Integration-Event)                 */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->publish_domain_event);\n    if (!cb->publish_domain_event(req, \"StipendDisbursed\", err_out)) {\n\n        /* Compensation Path #3: ledger reversal + reverse transfer + release budget */\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->record_ledger_entry);\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->reverse_transfer);\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->release_budget);\n\n        saga_error_t cmp_err = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n        cb->record_ledger_entry(req, \"STIPEND_DISBURSEMENT_REVERSED\", network_tx_id, &cmp_err);\n        cb->reverse_transfer(network_tx_id, &cmp_err);\n        cb->release_budget(reservation_id, &cmp_err);\n\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 6. Success!                                                        */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    if (err_out) {\n        *err_out = SAGA_ERROR_INIT(); /* reset to success */\n    }\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Example: Default No-Op Callbacks for Unit-Testing                         */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n#ifdef EDUPAY_STIPEND_SAGA_ENABLE_NOOP_CALLBACKS\n\n#include <string.h>\n\n/* These compile-time helpers allow professors to run the saga in a REPL\n * without wiring external systems.  Each callback prints to stdout and\n * pretends to succeed.\n */\n\nstatic inline bool noop_validate(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] validate_eligibility\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_reserve(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n                                uint64_t *id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] reserve_budget\");\n    *id = 42;\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_release(uint64_t id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)id; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] release_budget\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_transfer(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n                                 uint64_t *id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] initiate_transfer\");\n    *id = 1337;\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_reverse(uint64_t id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)id; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] reverse_transfer\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_ledger(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n                               const char *type, uint64_t rel_id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)type; (void)rel_id; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] record_ledger_entry\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_publish(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n                                const char *name, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)name; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] publish_domain_event\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic const stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t STIPEND_SAGA_NOOP_CALLBACKS = {\n    .validate_eligibility = noop_validate,\n    .reserve_budget       = noop_reserve,\n    .release_budget       = noop_release,\n    .initiate_transfer    = noop_transfer,\n    .reverse_transfer     = noop_reverse,\n    .record_ledger_entry  = noop_ledger,\n    .publish_domain_event = noop_publish\n};\n\n#endif /* EDUPAY_STIPEND_SAGA_ENABLE_NOOP_CALLBACKS */\n\n#endif /* EDUPAY_LEDGER_ACADEMY_FINANCIAL_AID_DISBURSE_STIPEND_SAGA_H */\n",

    "content": "```markdown\n# EduPay Ledger Academy  \n### docs/architecture/04_saga_pattern.md\n---\n> Version: 1.3  \n> Last Reviewed: 2024-05-09  \n> Authors: Core Platform Team (@edupay-ledger)  \n> Status: \u2705 Production  \n---\n\n## 1. Why EduPay Uses the Saga Pattern\n\nEduPay processes **millions of distributed, financial micro-transactions** each semester.  \nThe platform deliberately avoids *single-phase* database transactions because:\n\n* **Micro-services** compose payments from multiple bounded contexts (Admissions, Bursar, Treasury, FX, Fraud).  \n* **Heterogeneous data stores** (PostgreSQL, Redis, EventStoreDB) participate in a single business flow.  \n* **Resiliency labs** in coursework require controlled failure injection and roll-back.  \n\nA **Saga** slices a long-running business process into a series of *local* ACID transactions plus **compensating steps**.  \nIf any step fails, the orchestrator triggers rollback actions in **reverse order**, yielding *eventual consistency* without locking global resources.\n\n```\nEnrollment_Fee \u2192 FX_Conversion \u2192 Treasury_Posting \u2192 Fraud_Scoring \u2192 Receipt_Email\n         \u2502                \u2502                \u2502              \u2502\n         \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2534\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2534\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2534\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n                       Saga Orchestrator (payment_saga.c)       \u2502\n                       \u2022 persists state in Audit_Trail          \u2502\n                       \u2022 broadcasts events over EventBus        \u2502\n                       \u2022 drives rollbacks on failure \u25c4\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. High-Level Flow\n\n1. **Create** a `payment_saga_t` record in the `audit_trail` stream.  \n2. **Send** `SAGA_STEP_BEGIN` for *FX_Conversion* (`fx.c`).  \n3. **Local commit** in FX; publish `SAGA_STEP_DONE`.  \n4. Orchestrator continues to *Treasury_Posting* (`ledger.c`).  \n5. If *Fraud_Scoring* fails, **publish** `SAGA_ABORT`.  \n6. Participants receiving `SAGA_ABORT` invoke *compensating* handlers.  \n7. Saga ends with `SAGA_ROLLBACK_DONE` or `SAGA_SUCCESS`.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Reference Implementation (C)\n\nAll code is kept framework-agnostic, consistent with **Clean Architecture**.  \nDependencies limited to the standard C library (`pthread` for concurrency).\n\n### 3.1. Public Interface \u2013 `include/saga.h`\n\n```c\n#ifndef EDUPAY_SAGA_H\n#define EDUPAY_SAGA_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n\n/* ---------- Event Bus ---------------------------------------------------- */\n\ntypedef enum {\n    EVT_SAGA_STEP_BEGIN,\n    EVT_SAGA_STEP_DONE,\n    EVT_SAGA_ABORT,\n    EVT_SAGA_ROLLBACK_DONE,\n    EVT_SAGA_SUCCESS\n} saga_event_type_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    saga_event_type_t type;\n    uint64_t          saga_id;\n    const char       *step_name;   /* e.g., \"FX_Conversion\" */\n    void             *payload;     /* opaque domain state   */\n} saga_event_t;\n\n/* Subscriber callback signature */\ntypedef void (*event_handler_f)(const saga_event_t *evt, void *ctx);\n\n/* Registers a handler; returns 0 on success, -1 on error */\nint eventbus_subscribe(event_handler_f cb, void *ctx);\n\n/* Broadcasts event to all subscribers; thread-safe */\nint eventbus_publish(const saga_event_t *evt);\n\n/* ---------- Saga Orchestrator ------------------------------------------- */\n\n#define SAGA_MAX_STEPS 8\n#define SAGA_STEP_NAME_MAX 32\n\ntypedef int (*saga_step_f)(uint64_t saga_id, void **payload);\ntypedef int (*saga_comp_f)(uint64_t saga_id, void *payload);\n\ntypedef struct {\n    char         name[SAGA_STEP_NAME_MAX];\n    saga_step_f  action;\n    saga_comp_f  compensate;\n} saga_step_def_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    uint64_t        id;\n    uint8_t         step_count;\n    uint8_t         current;\n    saga_step_def_t steps[SAGA_MAX_STEPS];\n    bool            aborted;\n} payment_saga_t;\n\n/* Initializes a saga with the supplied steps */\nvoid saga_init(payment_saga_t *saga, uint64_t id,\n               const saga_step_def_t *steps,\n               uint8_t step_count);\n\n/* Executes saga synchronously; returns 0 on success, -1 on failure */\nint saga_execute(payment_saga_t *saga);\n\n#endif /* EDUPAY_SAGA_H */\n```\n\n### 3.2. Core Implementation \u2013 `src/saga.c`\n\n```c\n#include \"saga.h\"\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n\n#define BUS_MAX_HANDLERS 16\n\n/* ----------------- Simple In-Process Event Bus -------------------------- */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    event_handler_f cb;\n    void           *ctx;\n} handler_entry_t;\n\nstatic handler_entry_t BUS[BUS_MAX_HANDLERS];\nstatic pthread_mutex_t BUS_LOCK = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER;\n\nint eventbus_subscribe(event_handler_f cb, void *ctx)\n{\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&BUS_LOCK);\n    for (int i = 0; i < BUS_MAX_HANDLERS; ++i) {\n        if (BUS[i].cb == NULL) {\n            BUS[i].cb  = cb;\n            BUS[i].ctx = ctx;\n            pthread_mutex_unlock(&BUS_LOCK);\n            return 0;\n        }\n    }\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&BUS_LOCK);\n    return -1; /* No slots */\n}\n\nint eventbus_publish(const saga_event_t *evt)\n{\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&BUS_LOCK);\n    handler_entry_t handlers[BUS_MAX_HANDLERS];\n    memcpy(handlers, BUS, sizeof(handlers));\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&BUS_LOCK);\n\n    for (int i = 0; i < BUS_MAX_HANDLERS; ++i) {\n        if (handlers[i].cb)\n            handlers[i].cb(evt, handlers[i].ctx);\n    }\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* ----------------- Saga Orchestration ---------------------------------- */\n\nstatic void publish_step_event(saga_event_type_t type,\n                               const payment_saga_t *saga,\n                               const char *step_name,\n                               void *payload)\n{\n    saga_event_t evt = {\n        .type      = type,\n        .saga_id   = saga->id,\n        .step_name = step_name,\n        .payload   = payload\n    };\n    eventbus_publish(&evt);\n}\n\nvoid saga_init(payment_saga_t *s, uint64_t id,\n               const saga_step_def_t *steps,\n               uint8_t step_count)\n{\n    memset(s, 0, sizeof(*s));\n    s->id         = id;\n    s->step_count = step_count > SAGA_MAX_STEPS ? SAGA_MAX_STEPS : step_count;\n    memcpy(s->steps, steps, s->step_count * sizeof(saga_step_def_t));\n}\n\nstatic int rollback(payment_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    for (int i = saga->current; i >= 0; --i) {\n        saga_step_def_t *step = &saga->steps[i];\n        if (step->compensate) {\n            publish_step_event(EVT_SAGA_ABORT, saga, step->name, NULL);\n            if (step->compensate(saga->id, NULL) != 0)\n                fprintf(stderr, \"\u26a0  Compensation failed at %s\\n\", step->name);\n        }\n    }\n    saga_event_t done = {\n        .type      = EVT_SAGA_ROLLBACK_DONE,\n        .saga_id   = saga->id,\n        .step_name = \"ROLLBACK\"\n    };\n    eventbus_publish(&done);\n    return -1;\n}\n\nint saga_execute(payment_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    for (saga->current = 0; saga->current < saga->step_count; ++saga->current) {\n        saga_step_def_t *step = &saga->steps[saga->current];\n\n        publish_step_event(EVT_SAGA_STEP_BEGIN, saga, step->name, NULL);\n\n        void *payload = NULL;\n        if (step->action(saga->id, &payload) != 0) {\n            fprintf(stderr, \"\u274c  Saga %lu failed at step %s\\n\",\n                    saga->id, step->name);\n            saga->aborted = true;\n            return rollback(saga);\n        }\n\n        publish_step_event(EVT_SAGA_STEP_DONE, saga, step->name, payload);\n    }\n\n    saga_event_t ok = {\n        .type      = EVT_SAGA_SUCCESS,\n        .saga_id   = saga->id,\n        .step_name = \"COMPLETED\"\n    };\n    eventbus_publish(&ok);\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3. Example Steps \u2013 `src/steps_fx.c`, `src/steps_ledger.c`\n\n```c\n/* src/steps_fx.c */\n#include \"saga.h\"\n#include <stdio.h>\n\nint fx_convert(uint64_t id, void **payload)\n{\n    (void)payload; /* Not needed for demo */\n    printf(\"\ud83d\udcb1  FX_Conversion performed for saga %lu\\n\", id);\n    /* simulate success */\n    return 0;\n}\n\nint fx_reverse(uint64_t id, void *payload)\n{\n    (void)payload;\n    printf(\"\u21a9  FX_Conversion reversed for saga %lu\\n\", id);\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\n```c\n/* src/steps_ledger.c */\n#include \"saga.h\"\n#include <stdio.h>\n\nint ledger_post(uint64_t id, void **payload)\n{\n    (void)payload;\n    printf(\"\ud83d\udcd2  Ledger posting OK for saga %lu\\n\", id);\n    return 0;\n}\n\nint ledger_reverse(uint64_t id, void *payload)\n{\n    (void)payload;\n    printf(\"\u21a9  Ledger posting reversed for saga %lu\\n\", id);\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\n### 3.4. Demonstration Driver \u2013 `samples/payment_saga.c`\n\n```c\n#include \"saga.h\"\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n/* ---------- Step Implementations --------------------------------------- */\nextern int fx_convert(uint64_t, void **);\nextern int fx_reverse(uint64_t, void *);\n\nextern int ledger_post(uint64_t, void **);\nextern int ledger_reverse(uint64_t, void *);\n\nstatic int fraud_score(uint64_t id, void **payload)\n{\n    (void)payload;\n    printf(\"\ud83d\udd75  Fraud scoring started for saga %lu\\n\", id);\n\n    /* Simulate 30% failure rate for classroom chaos monkeys */\n    if (rand() % 10 < 3) {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"\ud83d\udea8  Fraud scoring FAILED (suspicious)\\n\");\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    printf(\"\u2705  Fraud scoring passed\\n\");\n    return 0;\n}\n\nstatic int fraud_reverse(uint64_t id, void *payload)\n{\n    (void)payload;\n    printf(\"\u21a9  Fraud scoring compensation (unflag) for saga %lu\\n\", id);\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* ---------- Audit Trail Console Subscriber ----------------------------- */\nstatic void audit_logger(const saga_event_t *evt, void *ctx)\n{\n    (void)ctx;\n    const char *type_str[] = {\n        \"STEP_BEGIN\", \"STEP_DONE\", \"ABORT\", \"ROLLBACK_DONE\", \"SUCCESS\"\n    };\n    printf(\"\ud83d\udcdd  Audit: %s \u2014 saga=%lu step=%s\\n\",\n           type_str[evt->type], evt->saga_id, evt->step_name);\n}\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    srand((unsigned)time(NULL));\n    eventbus_subscribe(audit_logger, NULL);\n\n    saga_step_def_t steps[] = {\n        { \"FX_Conversion\",   fx_convert,   fx_reverse   },\n        { \"Ledger_Posting\",  ledger_post,  ledger_reverse },\n        { \"Fraud_Scoring\",   fraud_score,  fraud_reverse }\n    };\n\n    payment_saga_t saga;\n    saga_init(&saga, 42, steps, 3);\n\n    int rc = saga_execute(&saga);\n    printf(rc == 0 ? \"\ud83c\udf89  Saga completed successfully!\\n\"\n                   : \"\ud83d\udc94  Saga rolled back.\\n\");\n    return rc;\n}\n```\n\nCompile & Run:\n\n```bash\ngcc -Iinclude src/saga.c src/steps_fx.c src/steps_ledger.c samples/payment_saga.c -lpthread -o bin/payment_saga\n./bin/payment_saga\n```\n\nExpected terminal output (with occasional induced failure):\n\n```\n\ud83d\udcb1  FX_Conversion performed for saga 42\n\ud83d\udcd2  Ledger posting OK for saga 42\n\ud83d\udd75  Fraud scoring started for saga 42\n\ud83d\udea8  Fraud scoring FAILED (suspicious)\n\u274c  Saga 42 failed at step Fraud_Scoring\n\u21a9  Fraud scoring compensation (unflag) for saga 42\n\u21a9  Ledger posting reversed for saga 42\n\u21a9  FX_Conversion reversed for saga 42\n\ud83d\udc94  Saga rolled back.\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Teaching Notes\n\n* The orchestrator resides **inside** the Payment bounded context, not in an external workflow engine.  \n  Code can therefore be debugged with `gdb` by novices.\n* Because the event bus is *in-process*, instructors can swap it for a\n  real Kafka / NATS adapter during advanced labs without touching business logic.\n* Compensations are **idempotent**: every reverse handler can run twice safely,\n  a mandatory property in at-least-once delivery environments.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Production Hardening Checklist\n\n- [x] Persist `payment_saga_t` progress to EventStoreDB \u2192 replay after crash.  \n- [x] Encrypt payloads (`payload_encrypt()`) for PCI-DSS compliance.  \n- [x] Emit OpenTelemetry spans for distributed tracing.  \n- [ ] Add circuit-breakers around downstream services (coming Q3).  \n\n---\n\nHappy hacking!  \nEduPay Ledger Team \u2728\n```",

Because the platform is intended both for **production payment flows** and for\n**pedagogical deep-dives**, every security control is written in C with pristine readability,\nstrong encapsulation, and complete unit-test coverage.\n\nThis document serves three audiences:\n\n1. **C-level security engineers** hardening live campus deployments.  \n2. **Professors & students** dissecting real-world fintech counter-measures.  \n3. **Auditors (PCI-DSS, SOC 2, FERPA, PSD2)** reviewing our design artifacts.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Threat Model\n\n| Asset                          | Adversary Goal                          | Mitigation                                                                             |\n| ------------------------------ | --------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |\n| Cardholder data (CHD)          | Exfiltrate PANs, CVVs, expiry dates     | Tokenization, AES-256-GCM at rest, TLS 1.3 in flight, mlock/munlock secrets            |\n| Tuition escrow accounts        | Unauthorized payout or diversion        | Dual-signature ledger, role-based ACL, multi-factor TOTP                               |\n| Student PII (FERPA)            | Deanonymize academic records            | Record-level field encryption, Attribute-based access control (ABAC)                   |\n| Audit logs                     | Tamper with or delete evidence          | Append-only Event Store, HMAC-SHA-256 chain-linking                                    |\n| Sagas (distributed txns)       | Replay or reorder compensating actions  | Idempotent command IDs, monotonic vector clocks                                        |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Regulatory Compliance Matrix\n\n| Regulation | Relevant ELA Module(s)                       | Key Controls Implemented                                                                     |\n| ---------- | -------------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |\n| PCI-DSS 4  | `pci_tokenizer`, `tls_terminator`, `vault`   | PAN truncation, secure memory, quarterly ASV scans, FIPS 140-2 crypto                        |\n| PSD2       | `strong_customer_auth`, `risk_engine`        | SCA 2-factor routing, dynamic linking of transaction data                                    |\n| SOC 2 TSC  | `audit_trail`, `config_service`              | Immutable logs, least-privilege secrets rotation                                             |\n| FERPA      | `pii_encryptor`, `reporting_gateway`         | Field-level AES, consent enforcement, purpose-based de-identification                        |\n\n---\n\n## 3. Reference Implementation: PCI Tokenization Service\nThe code below is **production-ready** and compiles as a standalone library.  It demonstrates:\n\n* FIPS-compatible AES-256-GCM encryption\n* High-entropy random token generation\n* Memory-safe key handling with `mlock` + `OPENSSL_cleanse`\n* Audit-ready error codes\n\n> File location in repo: `src/security/pci_tokenizer.c`\n\n```c\n/**\n * @file pci_tokenizer.c\n *\n * Production-grade PAN tokenization compliant with PCI-DSS 4.\n *\n * Build:\n *   gcc -Wall -Wextra -Werror -pedantic -std=c11 \\\n *       pci_tokenizer.c -o libpci_tokenizer.so -fPIC -shared -lcrypto\n *\n * Author: EduPay Ledger Academy Security Team\n */\n\n#include <errno.h>\n#include <inttypes.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stddef.h>\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include <sys/mman.h>\n#include <unistd.h>\n\n#include <openssl/evp.h>\n#include <openssl/rand.h>\n#include <openssl/err.h>\n\n/* \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 Public Constants \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 */\n#define PCI_TOKENIZER_OK                 (0)\n#define PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_CRYPTO        (-1)\n#define PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_RNG           (-2)\n#define PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_PARAM         (-3)\n#define PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_INTERNAL      (-4)\n\n/* Always tokenise PAN down to 16 random hex chars */\n#define TOKEN_LEN_HEX                   (16)\n\n/* AES-256-GCM parameters */\n#define AES_GCM_KEY_BYTES               (32)\n#define AES_GCM_IV_BYTES                (12)\n#define AES_GCM_TAG_BYTES               (16)\n\n/* Compile-time checks */\n#if TOKEN_LEN_HEX % 2 != 0\n#   error \"TOKEN_LEN_HEX must be divisible by 2\"\n#endif\n\n/* \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 Secure Utilities \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 */\n\n/**\n * Allocate memory that is locked into RAM, never swapped to disk.\n * Returns NULL on failure.\n */\nstatic void *secure_calloc(size_t n, size_t size) {\n    size_t total = n * size;\n    void *ptr = calloc(1, total);\n    if (!ptr) return NULL;\n\n    if (mlock(ptr, total) != 0) {\n        /* Best-effort fallback: continue even if mlock fails on some OS */\n        perror(\"mlock\");\n    }\n    return ptr;\n}\n\n/**\n * Frees memory allocated by secure_calloc, wiping contents first.\n */\nstatic void secure_free(void *ptr, size_t bytes) {\n    if (!ptr) return;\n    OPENSSL_cleanse(ptr, bytes);\n    munlock(ptr, bytes);\n    free(ptr);\n}\n\n/* \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 Core API \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 */\n\n/**\n * Generates a cryptographically strong random hex string of TOKEN_LEN_HEX.\n */\nstatic int generate_token(char token_out[TOKEN_LEN_HEX + 1]) {\n    uint8_t raw[TOKEN_LEN_HEX / 2];\n    if (RAND_bytes(raw, sizeof(raw)) != 1) {\n        return PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_RNG;\n    }\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < sizeof(raw); ++i)\n        sprintf(&token_out[i * 2], \"%02x\", raw[i]);\n\n    token_out[TOKEN_LEN_HEX] = '\\0';\n    return PCI_TOKENIZER_OK;\n}\n\n/**\n * Encrypts plaintext using AES-256-GCM.\n *\n * Inputs:\n *   key:        32-byte key\n *   iv:         12-byte IV\n *   plaintext:  PAN string\n *   pt_len:     plaintext length in bytes\n *\n * Outputs:\n *   ciphertext: caller-allocated buffer at least pt_len bytes\n *   tag:        16-byte authentication tag\n *   ct_len:     actual number of ciphertext bytes written\n *\n * Returns PCI_TOKENIZER_* status code.\n */\nstatic int aes256_gcm_encrypt(const uint8_t key[AES_GCM_KEY_BYTES],\n                              const uint8_t iv[AES_GCM_IV_BYTES],\n                              const uint8_t *plaintext,\n                              size_t pt_len,\n                              uint8_t *ciphertext,\n                              uint8_t tag[AES_GCM_TAG_BYTES],\n                              size_t *ct_len) {\n\n    EVP_CIPHER_CTX *ctx = EVP_CIPHER_CTX_new();\n    if (!ctx) return PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_CRYPTO;\n\n    int len = 0;\n    int ciphertext_len = 0;\n    int ret_code = PCI_TOKENIZER_OK;\n\n    do {\n        if (EVP_EncryptInit_ex(ctx, EVP_aes_256_gcm(), NULL, NULL, NULL) != 1) {\n            ret_code = PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_CRYPTO; break;\n        }\n        if (EVP_CIPHER_CTX_ctrl(ctx, EVP_CTRL_GCM_SET_IVLEN, AES_GCM_IV_BYTES, NULL) != 1) {\n            ret_code = PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_CRYPTO; break;\n        }\n        if (EVP_EncryptInit_ex(ctx, NULL, NULL, key, iv) != 1) {\n            ret_code = PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_CRYPTO; break;\n        }\n        if (EVP_EncryptUpdate(ctx, ciphertext, &len, plaintext, (int)pt_len) != 1) {\n            ret_code = PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_CRYPTO; break;\n        }\n        ciphertext_len = len;\n        if (EVP_EncryptFinal_ex(ctx, ciphertext + len, &len) != 1) {\n            ret_code = PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_CRYPTO; break;\n        }\n        ciphertext_len += len;\n        if (EVP_CIPHER_CTX_ctrl(ctx, EVP_CTRL_GCM_GET_TAG, AES_GCM_TAG_BYTES, tag) != 1) {\n            ret_code = PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_CRYPTO; break;\n        }\n        *ct_len = (size_t)ciphertext_len;\n    } while (0);\n\n    EVP_CIPHER_CTX_free(ctx);\n    if (ret_code != PCI_TOKENIZER_OK)\n        ERR_print_errors_fp(stderr);\n\n    return ret_code;\n}\n\n/* \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 Public Facade \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 */\n\n/**\n * Tokenises a Primary Account Number (PAN).\n *\n * The caller supplies:\n *   pan                 PAN string (digits only)\n *\n * The library returns:\n *   out_token           TOKEN_LEN_HEX-char hex string\n *   out_ciphertext      Encrypted PAN (malloc'd, must be free()'d by caller)\n *   out_ciphertext_len  Length of encrypted PAN\n *   out_iv              12-byte IV\n *   out_tag             16-byte GCM tag\n *\n * Note: the encryption key is managed by the HSM module; for demo purposes\n *       we generate a random key here and return it to the caller.\n */\nint pci_tokenize_pan(const char  *pan,\n                     char        out_token[TOKEN_LEN_HEX + 1],\n                     uint8_t   **out_ciphertext,\n                     size_t     *out_ciphertext_len,\n                     uint8_t     out_iv[AES_GCM_IV_BYTES],\n                     uint8_t     out_tag[AES_GCM_TAG_BYTES],\n                     uint8_t     out_key[AES_GCM_KEY_BYTES]) {\n\n    if (!pan || !out_token || !out_ciphertext || !out_ciphertext_len ||\n        !out_iv || !out_tag || !out_key) {\n        return PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_PARAM;\n    }\n\n    size_t pan_len = strlen(pan);\n    if (pan_len == 0 || pan_len > 32) { /* 19 digits + possible separators */\n        return PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_PARAM;\n    }\n\n    /* Step 1: generate random token */\n    int rc = generate_token(out_token);\n    if (rc != PCI_TOKENIZER_OK) return rc;\n\n    /* Step 2: generate fresh AES GCM key & IV */\n    if (RAND_bytes(out_key, AES_GCM_KEY_BYTES) != 1) {\n        return PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_RNG;\n    }\n    if (RAND_bytes(out_iv, AES_GCM_IV_BYTES) != 1) {\n        return PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_RNG;\n    }\n\n    /* Step 3: secure memory allocation for ciphertext */\n    *out_ciphertext = malloc(pan_len); /* ciphertext length equals plaintext */\n    if (!*out_ciphertext) {\n        return PCI_TOKENIZER_ERR_INTERNAL;\n    }\n\n    /* Step 4: encrypt PAN */\n    rc = aes256_gcm_encrypt(out_key,\n                            out_iv,\n                            (const uint8_t *)pan,\n                            pan_len,\n                            *out_ciphertext,\n                            out_tag,\n                            out_ciphertext_len);\n\n    if (rc != PCI_TOKENIZER_OK) {\n        OPENSSL_cleanse(*out_ciphertext, pan_len);\n        free(*out_ciphertext);\n        *out_ciphertext = NULL;\n        *out_ciphertext_len = 0;\n        return rc;\n    }\n\n    return PCI_TOKENIZER_OK;\n}\n\n/**\n * Wipes and frees the ciphertext buffer returned by pci_tokenize_pan().\n */\nvoid pci_tokenizer_free_ciphertext(uint8_t *ciphertext, size_t len) {\n    if (!ciphertext) return;\n    OPENSSL_cleanse(ciphertext, len);\n    free(ciphertext);\n}\n\n/* \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 Example Usage \u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014\u2014 */\n#ifdef PCI_TOKENIZER_DEMO_MAIN\nint main(void) {\n    const char *pan = \"4111111111111111\";\n    char token[TOKEN_LEN_HEX + 1];\n\n    uint8_t *ciphertext = NULL;\n    size_t   ciphertext_len = 0;\n    uint8_t  iv[AES_GCM_IV_BYTES];\n    uint8_t  tag[AES_GCM_TAG_BYTES];\n    uint8_t  key[AES_GCM_KEY_BYTES];\n\n    int rc = pci_tokenize_pan(pan, token, &ciphertext, &ciphertext_len,\n                              iv, tag, key);\n    if (rc != PCI_TOKENIZER_OK) {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"Tokenization failed (err=%d)\\n\", rc);\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    printf(\"PAN           : %s\\n\", pan);\n    printf(\"Token         : %s\\n\", token);\n    printf(\"Ciphertext    : \");\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < ciphertext_len; ++i)\n        printf(\"%02x\", ciphertext[i]);\n    printf(\"\\n\");\n\n    /* Proper key handling omitted for brevity \u2014 would be escrowed in HSM. */\n    pci_tokenizer_free_ciphertext(ciphertext, ciphertext_len);\n    OPENSSL_cleanse(key, sizeof(key));\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n#endif\n```\n\n### Unit Test Snippet\n\n```c\n#include \"pci_tokenizer.h\"\n#include <assert.h>\n\nvoid test_token_length(void) {\n    char token[TOKEN_LEN_HEX + 1];\n    /* ... invoke tokenizer ... */\n    assert(strlen(token) == TOKEN_LEN_HEX);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Additional Controls & Roadmap\n\n1. **Runtime ASLR Enforcement** \u2013 `seccomp` + clang CFI flags.  \n2. **Key Rotation Service** \u2013 Zero-downtime re-encryption of vault rows.  \n3. **FIDO2 WebAuthn** \u2013 Replacing TOTP for privileged bursar operations.  \n4. **Continuous Compliance** \u2013 Open Policy Agent (OPA) integration for FERPA audits.  \n\n---\n\n## 5. All functions are\n  synchronous and fail-fast; wrap them in your platform\u2019s preferred error\n  handling and tracing facilities when deploying in production.\n\n  Build note: link with -lcrypto (OpenSSL 1.1.1+) or LibreSSL 3.x.\n\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500*/\n#ifndef EDU_COMPLIANCE_GUARD_H\n#define EDU_COMPLIANCE_GUARD_H\n\n#include <stddef.h>   /* size_t   */\n#include <stdint.h>   /* uint8_t  */\n#include <stdbool.h>  /* bool     */\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\nextern \"C\" {\n#endif\n\n/* Opaque symmetric-key handle \u2011 see cg_key_acquire() */\ntypedef struct cg_key cg_key_t;\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  PCI-DSS Safe Tokenisation                                                */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Generates a numeric, Luhn-valid token that preserves the first six\n * digits (BIN/IIN) of the supplied Primary Account Number.\n *\n * The function is idempotent; identical input produces identical output\n * when `EDUPAY_FPE=0`.  Set `EDUPAY_FPE=1` to switch to format-preserving\n * encryption (left as an exercise).\n *\n * Memory safety: the caller owns both the input PAN and output buffer.\n * Call cg_secure_bzero() after use.\n *\n * @return 0 on success, \u2011EINVAL on bad input, negative errno on failure.\n */\nint cg_tokenise_pan(const char *pan,\n                    char       *out_token,\n                    size_t      out_len);\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Authenticated Encryption (AES-256-GCM)                                   */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Encrypts |plaintext| and prepends a random IV, appending a 128-bit tag.\n *\n * |out_cipher| must be at least 12 B + pt_len + 16 B.\n * Returns total bytes written or negative errno.\n */\nssize_t cg_seal(cg_key_t      *key,\n                const uint8_t *plaintext,\n                size_t         pt_len,\n                uint8_t       *out_cipher,\n                size_t         out_cipher_sz);\n\n/**\n * Decrypts and authenticates a buffer produced by cg_seal().\n *\n * Returns number of plaintext bytes or \u2011EBADMSG when auth fails.\n */\nssize_t cg_open(cg_key_t      *key,\n                const uint8_t *cipher,\n                size_t         cipher_len,\n                uint8_t       *out_plain,\n                size_t         out_plain_sz);\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Secure memory hygiene                                                    */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/* Overwrite |len| bytes starting at |ptr| even under aggressive optimisation */\nvoid cg_secure_bzero(void *ptr, size_t len);\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Key management (teaching mode)                                           */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Acquires an AES-256-GCM key.\n *   \u2022 Production:  pulled from HSM via PKCS#11.\n *   \u2022 Lab mode:    derived from EDUPAY_COMPLIANCE_KEY (64-hex chars) or\n *                  filled with /dev/urandom.\n */\ncg_key_t *cg_key_acquire(void);\n\n/* Zeroise and free key material */\nvoid cg_key_release(cg_key_t *key);\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\n}\n#endif\n#endif /* EDU_COMPLIANCE_GUARD_H */\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2 \u2571 4\u2003Reference implementation (`compliance_guard.c`)\n\n```c\n/*\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n  compliance_guard.c  \u2014  Internal library for the Compliance micro-service\n\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500*/\n#include \"compliance_guard.h\"\n\n#include <openssl/evp.h>\n#include <openssl/rand.h>\n#include <errno.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n\n#define CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN   12u\n#define CG_AES_GCM_TAG_LEN  16u\n#define CG_PAN_MAX_LEN      19u     /* ISO/IEC 7812-1 */\n#define CG_TOKEN_LEN        19u\n\nstruct cg_key { uint8_t key[32]; };\n\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 Internal helpers \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n\nstatic int cg_generate_iv(uint8_t *iv, size_t iv_len)\n{\n    return RAND_bytes(iv, (int)iv_len) == 1 ? 0 : -EIO;\n}\n\nstatic int cg_validate_luhn(const char *digits)\n{\n    size_t len = strlen(digits);\n    int sum = 0, alt = 0;\n\n    for (ssize_t i = (ssize_t)len - 1; i >= 0; --i)\n    {\n        int d = digits[i] - '0';\n        if (d < 0 || d > 9) return -EINVAL;\n        if (alt) { d *= 2; if (d > 9) d -= 9; }\n        sum += d; alt = !alt;\n    }\n    return sum % 10 == 0 ? 0 : -EINVAL;\n}\n\nstatic uint8_t cg_rand_digit(void)\n{\n    uint8_t b; RAND_bytes(&b, 1); return (uint8_t)(b % 10);\n}\n\nstatic int cg_build_token(const char *pan, char *tok)\n{\n    size_t len = strlen(pan);\n    if (len < 8 || len > CG_PAN_MAX_LEN) return -EINVAL;\n\n    memcpy(tok, pan, 6);                 /* Keep BIN for analytics */\n    for (size_t i = 6; i < len - 1; ++i) /* Randomise body         */\n        tok[i] = '0' + cg_rand_digit();\n\n    /* Recalculate Luhn check digit */\n    int sum = 0, alt = 1;\n    for (ssize_t i = (ssize_t)len - 2; i >= 0; --i)\n    {\n        int d = tok[i] - '0';\n        if (alt) { d *= 2; if (d > 9) d -= 9; }\n        sum += d; alt = !alt;\n    }\n    tok[len - 1] = '0' + ((10 - (sum % 10)) % 10);\n    tok[len] = '\\0';\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 Public API \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n\nint cg_tokenise_pan(const char *pan, char *out_token, size_t out_len)\n{\n    if (!pan || !out_token)                 return -EINVAL;\n    const size_t n = strlen(pan);\n    if (n == 0 || n > CG_PAN_MAX_LEN)       return -EINVAL;\n    if (out_len < n + 1)                    return -ENOSPC;\n    if (cg_validate_luhn(pan) != 0)         return -EINVAL;\n\n    /* Switchable algorithm for classroom demos */\n    if (getenv(\"EDUPAY_FPE\") && *getenv(\"EDUPAY_FPE\") == '1')\n    {\n        /* Placeholder for format-preserving AES-FF3-1 */\n        return cg_build_token(pan, out_token); /* Fallback path */\n    }\n    return cg_build_token(pan, out_token);\n}\n\nssize_t cg_seal(cg_key_t      *key,\n                const uint8_t *pt,\n                size_t         pt_len,\n                uint8_t       *out,\n                size_t         out_sz)\n{\n    if (!key || !pt || !out || pt_len == 0)  return -EINVAL;\n    const size_t need = CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN + pt_len + CG_AES_GCM_TAG_LEN;\n    if (out_sz < need)                       return -ENOSPC;\n\n    uint8_t *iv     = out;\n    uint8_t *cipher = out + CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN;\n    uint8_t *tag    = cipher + pt_len;\n\n    if (cg_generate_iv(iv, CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN) != 0) return -EIO;\n\n    ssize_t ret = -EIO;\n    EVP_CIPHER_CTX *ctx = EVP_CIPHER_CTX_new();\n    if (!ctx) return -ENOMEM;\n\n    do {\n        if (EVP_EncryptInit_ex(ctx, EVP_aes_256_gcm(), NULL, NULL, NULL) != 1) break;\n        if (EVP_CIPHER_CTX_ctrl(ctx, EVP_CTRL_GCM_SET_IVLEN,\n                                CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN, NULL) != 1)               break;\n        if (EVP_EncryptInit_ex(ctx, NULL, NULL, key->key, iv) != 1)           break;\n\n        int len = 0, total = 0;\n        if (EVP_EncryptUpdate(ctx, cipher, &len, pt, (int)pt_len) != 1)       break;\n        total += len;\n        if (EVP_EncryptFinal_ex(ctx, cipher + total, &len) != 1)              break;\n        total += len;\n        if (EVP_CIPHER_CTX_ctrl(ctx, EVP_CTRL_GCM_GET_TAG,\n                                CG_AES_GCM_TAG_LEN, tag) != 1)               break;\n\n        ret = CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN + total + CG_AES_GCM_TAG_LEN;\n    } while (0);\n\n    EVP_CIPHER_CTX_free(ctx);\n    return ret;\n}\n\nssize_t cg_open(cg_key_t      *key,\n                const uint8_t *in,\n                size_t         in_len,\n                uint8_t       *out,\n                size_t         out_sz)\n{\n    if (!key || !in || !out)                         return -EINVAL;\n    if (in_len < CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN + CG_AES_GCM_TAG_LEN) return -EINVAL;\n\n    const uint8_t *iv     = in;\n    const uint8_t *cipher = in + CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN;\n    const size_t   ct_len = in_len - CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN - CG_AES_GCM_TAG_LEN;\n    const uint8_t *tag    = in + in_len - CG_AES_GCM_TAG_LEN;\n\n    if (out_sz < ct_len)                             return -ENOSPC;\n\n    ssize_t ret = -EIO;\n    EVP_CIPHER_CTX *ctx = EVP_CIPHER_CTX_new();\n    if (!ctx) return -ENOMEM;\n\n    do {\n        if (EVP_DecryptInit_ex(ctx, EVP_aes_256_gcm(), NULL, NULL, NULL) != 1) break;\n        if (EVP_CIPHER_CTX_ctrl(ctx, EVP_CTRL_GCM_SET_IVLEN,\n                                CG_AES_GCM_IV_LEN, NULL) != 1)               break;\n        if (EVP_DecryptInit_ex(ctx, NULL, NULL, key->key, iv) != 1)           break;\n\n        int len = 0, total = 0;\n        if (EVP_DecryptUpdate(ctx, out, &len, cipher, (int)ct_len) != 1)      break;\n        total += len;\n\n        if (EVP_CIPHER_CTX_ctrl(ctx, EVP_CTRL_GCM_SET_TAG,\n                                CG_AES_GCM_TAG_LEN, (void *)tag) != 1)       break;\n        if (EVP_DecryptFinal_ex(ctx, out + total, &len) != 1) {\n            ret = -EBADMSG;                                                  break;\n        }\n        total += len;\n        ret = total;\n    } while (0);\n\n    EVP_CIPHER_CTX_free(ctx);\n    return ret;\n}\n\nvoid cg_secure_bzero(void *ptr, size_t len)\n{\n    if (!ptr || !len) return;\n#if defined(__STDC_LIB_EXT1__)\n    memset_s(ptr, len, 0, len);\n#else\n    volatile uint8_t *p = (volatile uint8_t *)ptr;\n    while (len--) *p++ = 0;\n#endif\n}\n\ncg_key_t *cg_key_acquire(void)\n{\n    cg_key_t *k = calloc(1, sizeof *k);\n    if (!k) return NULL;\n\n    const char *env = getenv(\"EDUPAY_COMPLIANCE_KEY\");\n    if (env && strlen(env) == 64)\n    {   /* Hex-decode deterministic, instructor-supplied key */\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < 32; ++i)\n            sscanf(&env[i * 2], \"%2hhx\", &k->key[i]);\n    }\n    else if (RAND_bytes(k->key, sizeof k->key) != 1)\n    {\n        free(k); k = NULL;\n    }\n    return k;\n}\n\nvoid cg_key_release(cg_key_t *key)\n{\n    if (!key) return;\n    cg_secure_bzero(key->key, sizeof key->key);\n    free(key);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3 \u2571 4\u2003End-to-end console demo (`example_usage.c`)\n\n```c\n/* Compile with\n *   cc -std=c11 -Wall -Wextra example_usage.c compliance_guard.c -lcrypto -o demo\n * Run with\n *   EDUPAY_COMPLIANCE_KEY=$(openssl rand -hex 32) ./demo\n */\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <string.h>\n\n#include \"compliance_guard.h\"\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    const char *pan = \"4485275742308327\"; /* Visa test card */\n\n    char token[CG_TOKEN_LEN + 1];\n    if (cg_tokenise_pan(pan, token, sizeof token) != 0) {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"Tokenisation failed\\n\");\n        return 1;\n    }\n    printf(\"Tokenised PAN  : %s\\n\", token);\n\n    cg_key_t *key = cg_key_acquire();\n    if (!key) { perror(\"key_acquire\"); return 1; }\n\n    uint8_t cipher[256];\n    ssize_t n_cipher = cg_seal(key,\n                               (const uint8_t *)token, strlen(token),\n                               cipher, sizeof cipher);\n    cg_secure_bzero(token, sizeof token); /* Immediately destroy clear-text */\n    if (n_cipher < 0) {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"Encryption failed: %zd\\n\", n_cipher);\n        cg_key_release(key);\n        return 1;\n    }\n\n    uint8_t clear[64];\n    ssize_t n_plain = cg_open(key, cipher, (size_t)n_cipher,\n                              clear, sizeof clear);\n    cg_key_release(key);\n\n    if (n_plain < 0) {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"Decryption failed: %zd\\n\", n_plain);\n        return 1;\n    }\n    printf(\"Decrypted token: %.*s\\n\", (int)n_plain, clear);\n    cg_secure_bzero(clear, (size_t)n_plain);\n\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4 \u2571 4\u2003Lab exercises\n\n1. Extend `cg_tokenise_pan()` to call an FF3-1 library when `EDUPAY_FPE=1`.  \n   Verify that the output still passes Luhn and preserves BIN/IIN.\n\n2. Attach `cg_seal()` to the CQRS \u2192 Audit-Trail write model.  \n   Use Wireshark to confirm that events on the message bus no longer contain\n   clear-text PAN or student identifiers (FERPA \u00a799.31).\n\n3. Fire up `valgrind --tool=memcheck ./demo` and inspect the heap after\n   `cg_secure_bzero()` executes. No clear-text secrets should appear.\n\n---\n\n\u00a9 2024 EduPay Ledger Academy \u2014 MIT License",

*/\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\nextern \"C\" {\n#endif\n\n/* Ledger event types that the projector knows how to fold.                  */\ntypedef enum\n{\n    EVT_UNDEFINED = 0,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_PROCESSED,\n    EVT_TRANSACTION_SETTLED,\n    EVT_FRAUD_FLAGGED,\n    EVT_CURRENCY_CONVERTED,\n    EVT_SCHOLARSHIP_DISBURSED\n} ledger_event_type_t;\n\n/* Immutable envelope received from the event-store / broker.                */\ntypedef struct\n{\n    ledger_event_type_t type;      /* Event discriminator.                  */\n    const char         *payload;   /* UTF-8 JSON blob (null-terminated).    */\n    uint64_t            sequence;  /* Global ordering, monotonic.           */\n    uint64_t            ts_epoch_ms; /* Milliseconds since Unix epoch.      */\n} ledger_event_t;\n\n/* Opaque handle exposed to application code.                                */\ntypedef struct\n{\n    sqlite3        *db;            /* Connection to read-model store.       */\n    pthread_mutex_t mtx;           /* Serializes concurrent folds.          */\n} dashboard_projector_t;\n\n/* Construction / teardown.  On failure, an explanatory message is written\n * to `stderr` and false is returned.                                        */\nbool dashboard_projector_init(dashboard_projector_t *prj,\n                              const char            *sqlite_path);\n\nvoid dashboard_projector_shutdown(dashboard_projector_t *prj);\n\n/* Fold a single ledger event into the dashboard read-model.  Thread-safe\n * (internally synchronized).                                                */\nvoid dashboard_projector_handle_event(dashboard_projector_t *prj,\n                                      const ledger_event_t  *evt);\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\n}\n#endif\n\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n/*  Inline Implementation                                                    */\n/* \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n\n#ifdef DASHBOARD_PROJECTOR_IMPLEMENTATION\n#error \"DASHBOARD_PROJECTOR_IMPLEMENTATION already defined elsewhere\"\n#endif\n#define DASHBOARD_PROJECTOR_IMPLEMENTATION 1\n\n/* SQLite helpers \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n\nstatic inline void _log_sqlite_error(const char *ctx, sqlite3 *db)\n{\n    fprintf(stderr, \"[dashboard_projector] %s: %s (code=%d)\\n\",\n            ctx, sqlite3_errmsg(db), sqlite3_errcode(db));\n}\n\nstatic inline bool _exec(sqlite3 *db, const char *sql)\n{\n    char *errmsg = NULL;\n    if (sqlite3_exec(db, sql, NULL, NULL, &errmsg) != SQLITE_OK)\n    {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"[dashboard_projector] SQL error: %s\\n\", errmsg);\n        sqlite3_free(errmsg);\n        return false;\n    }\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* Schema bootstrap \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n\nstatic const char *_DDL[] = {\n    /* Metadata used for idempotent re-playing (at-least-once deliveries).   */\n    \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projection_metadata (\"\n    \"  id                INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK (id = 1),\"\n    \"  last_sequence     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0\"\n    \");\"\n    \"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO projection_metadata (id, last_sequence) VALUES (1, 0);\",\n\n    /* Highly-denormalized table powering the dashboard widgets.             */\n    \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS dashboard_snapshot (\"\n    \"  id                  INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK (id = 1),\"\n    \"  total_payments_usd  REAL    NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,\"\n    \"  total_settlements   REAL    NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,\"\n    \"  fraud_incidents     INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\"\n    \"  scholarship_outflow REAL    NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0\"\n    \");\"\n    \"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO dashboard_snapshot (id) VALUES (1);\",\n\n    NULL /* sentinel */\n};\n\nstatic inline bool _ensure_schema(sqlite3 *db)\n{\n    for (const char **ddl = _DDL; *ddl; ++ddl)\n        if (!_exec(db, *ddl))\n            return false;\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* Primitive JSON parsing utilities (no external dependency).                */\n/* Security: Not a full JSON parser \u2014 good enough for our limited shapes.    */\n\nstatic inline bool _json_extract_double(const char *json,\n                                        const char *key,\n                                        double     *out_val)\n{\n    if (!json || !key || !out_val) return false;\n\n    const size_t key_len = strlen(key);\n    const char  *pos     = json;\n    while ((pos = strstr(pos, key)))\n    {\n        pos += key_len;\n        /* Skip whitespace, colon, whitespace */\n        while (*pos && (*pos == ' ' || *pos == '\\t' || *pos == '\\n' ||\n                        *pos == '\\r' || *pos == ':'))\n            ++pos;\n        if (!*pos) break;\n\n        /* +/-? digits?. */\n        char *endptr = NULL;\n        errno = 0;\n        double val  = strtod(pos, &endptr);\n        if (endptr != pos && errno == 0)\n        {\n            *out_val = val;\n            return true;\n        }\n        /* Else: continue searching (false hit). */\n    }\n    return false;\n}\n\n/* Fetch last processed sequence to achieve idempotency.                     */\nstatic inline uint64_t _get_last_sequence(sqlite3 *db)\n{\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    uint64_t      seq  = 0;\n\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(db,\n                           \"SELECT last_sequence FROM projection_metadata \"\n                           \"WHERE id = 1;\",\n                           -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK)\n    {\n        if (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_ROW)\n            seq = (uint64_t)sqlite3_column_int64(stmt, 0);\n    }\n    else\n        _log_sqlite_error(\"_get_last_sequence/prepare\", db);\n\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return seq;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool _update_last_sequence(sqlite3 *db, uint64_t seq)\n{\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    bool          ok   = false;\n\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(db,\n                           \"UPDATE projection_metadata SET last_sequence = ?\"\n                           \" WHERE id = 1;\",\n                           -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK)\n    {\n        sqlite3_bind_int64(stmt, 1, (sqlite3_int64)seq);\n        ok = (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_DONE);\n    }\n    else\n        _log_sqlite_error(\"_update_last_sequence/prepare\", db);\n\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return ok;\n}\n\n/* Public functions \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 */\n\nbool dashboard_projector_init(dashboard_projector_t *prj,\n                              const char            *sqlite_path)\n{\n    if (!prj || !sqlite_path)\n    {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"[dashboard_projector] init: invalid arguments\\n\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    memset(prj, 0, sizeof(*prj));\n\n    /* Open SQLite in WAL mode for concurrency friendliness.                 */\n    int rc = sqlite3_open_v2(sqlite_path,\n                             &prj->db,\n                             SQLITE_OPEN_READWRITE | SQLITE_OPEN_CREATE |\n                                 SQLITE_OPEN_FULLMUTEX,\n                             NULL);\n    if (rc != SQLITE_OK)\n    {\n        _log_sqlite_error(\"sqlite3_open_v2\", prj->db);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    if (!_ensure_schema(prj->db))\n        goto fail;\n\n    if (pthread_mutex_init(&prj->mtx, NULL) != 0)\n    {\n        fprintf(stderr, \"[dashboard_projector] pthread_mutex_init failed\\n\");\n        goto fail;\n    }\n\n    /* Switch to WAL for perf. */\n    if (!_exec(prj->db, \"PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;\"))\n        goto fail_mutex;\n\n    return true;\n\n/* Error unwind helpers */\nfail_mutex:\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&prj->mtx);\nfail:\n    sqlite3_close(prj->db);\n    prj->db = NULL;\n    return false;\n}\n\nvoid dashboard_projector_shutdown(dashboard_projector_t *prj)\n{\n    if (!prj || !prj->db) return;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&prj->mtx);\n    sqlite3_close(prj->db);\n    prj->db = NULL;\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&prj->mtx);\n\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&prj->mtx);\n}\n\n/* Actual fold implementation per event type.                                */\n\nstatic inline bool _fold_payment_processed(sqlite3 *db, double amount_usd)\n{\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    bool          ok   = false;\n\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(\n            db,\n            \"UPDATE dashboard_snapshot \"\n            \"SET total_payments_usd = total_payments_usd + ? \"\n            \"WHERE id = 1;\",\n            -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK)\n    {\n        sqlite3_bind_double(stmt, 1, amount_usd);\n        ok = (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_DONE);\n    }\n    else\n        _log_sqlite_error(\"_fold_payment_processed/prepare\", db);\n\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return ok;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool _fold_transaction_settled(sqlite3 *db, double amount)\n{\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    bool          ok   = false;\n\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(\n            db,\n            \"UPDATE dashboard_snapshot \"\n            \"SET total_settlements = total_settlements + ? \"\n            \"WHERE id = 1;\",\n            -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK)\n    {\n        sqlite3_bind_double(stmt, 1, amount);\n        ok = (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_DONE);\n    }\n    else\n        _log_sqlite_error(\"_fold_transaction_settled/prepare\", db);\n\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return ok;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool _fold_fraud_flagged(sqlite3 *db)\n{\n    return _exec(db,\n                 \"UPDATE dashboard_snapshot \"\n                 \"SET fraud_incidents = fraud_incidents + 1 \"\n                 \"WHERE id = 1;\");\n}\n\nstatic inline bool _fold_scholarship_disbursed(sqlite3 *db, double amount)\n{\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    bool          ok   = false;\n\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(\n            db,\n            \"UPDATE dashboard_snapshot \"\n            \"SET scholarship_outflow = scholarship_outflow + ? \"\n            \"WHERE id = 1;\",\n            -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK)\n    {\n        sqlite3_bind_double(stmt, 1, amount);\n        ok = (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_DONE);\n    }\n    else\n        _log_sqlite_error(\"_fold_scholarship_disbursed/prepare\", db);\n\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return ok;\n}\n\n/* Main folding orchestrator                                                 */\n\nvoid dashboard_projector_handle_event(dashboard_projector_t *prj,\n                                      const ledger_event_t  *evt)\n{\n    if (!prj || !evt || !prj->db) return;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&prj->mtx);\n\n    /* Idempotent replay guard.                                              */\n    uint64_t last_seq = _get_last_sequence(prj->db);\n    if (evt->sequence <= last_seq)\n    {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&prj->mtx);\n        return; /* Already processed. */\n    }\n\n    /* Begin transaction.                                                    */\n    if (!_exec(prj->db, \"BEGIN;\"))\n        goto unlock;\n\n    bool fold_ok  = false;\n    double amount = 0.0;\n\n    switch (evt->type)\n    {\n        case EVT_PAYMENT_PROCESSED:\n            if (_json_extract_double(evt->payload, \"\\\"amount\\\"\", &amount))\n                fold_ok = _fold_payment_processed(prj->db, amount);\n            break;\n\n        case EVT_TRANSACTION_SETTLED:\n            if (_json_extract_double(evt->payload, \"\\\"amount\\\"\", &amount))\n                fold_ok = _fold_transaction_settled(prj->db, amount);\n            break;\n\n        case EVT_FRAUD_FLAGGED:\n            fold_ok = _fold_fraud_flagged(prj->db);\n            break;\n\n        case EVT_SCHOLARSHIP_DISBURSED:\n            if (_json_extract_double(evt->payload, \"\\\"amount\\\"\", &amount))\n                fold_ok = _fold_scholarship_disbursed(prj->db, amount);\n            break;\n\n        /* Events not relevant for the dashboard are safely ignored.         */\n        default:\n            fold_ok = true;\n            break;\n    }\n\n    /* Update checkpoint if the fold succeeded.                              */\n    if (fold_ok)\n        fold_ok = _update_last_sequence(prj->db, evt->sequence);\n\n    /* Commit or rollback.                                                   */\n    if (fold_ok)\n    {\n        if (!_exec(prj->db, \"COMMIT;\"))\n            _exec(prj->db, \"ROLLBACK;\");\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        _exec(prj->db, \"ROLLBACK;\");\n    }\n\nunlock:\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&prj->mtx);\n}\n\n#endif /* EDUPAY_LEDGER_ACADEMY_DASHBOARD_PROJECTOR_H */\n",
