(clang \u2011std=c17 \u2011Wall \u2011Wextra\n-pedantic \u2011O2 listing.c \u2011o listing && ./listing)\n-->\n\n# Micro-services & Bounded Contexts\n\nEduPay Ledger Academy follows Domain-Driven Design and splits the\nbusiness domain into **four bounded contexts** (BCs).  Each BC is\nimplemented as one or more micro-services\u2014small autonomous executables\nwritten in C and packaged as OCI containers.\n\n| Bounded Context         | Canonical Service | Purpose                                                                    |\n|-------------------------|-------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------|\n| Admissions              | `admissions-api`  | On-boards students, allocates student-ids, emits *StudentRegistered*       |\n| Bursar (A/R)            | `ledger-core`     | Double-entry ledger, tuition invoicing, GL postings, payment gateway       |\n| Financial-Aid           | `aid-engine`      | Award rules, stipend disbursement, compliance (FERPA / PSD2 / PCI-DSS)     |\n| Continuing-Education    | `micro-cred`      | Per-course micro-credential tracking, pay-per-module split-payments         |\n\nA **Shared-Kernel** provides value-objects (`Money`, `Currency`,\n`StudentId`) and the **AuditTrail** event store.\n\n```\n                        +-----------+\n                        |  API-GW   |\n                        +-----------+\n                              |\n            +-----------------+------------------+\n            |                 |                  |\n    +--------------+  +---------------+  +---------------+\n    | admissions   |  | ledger-core   |  | aid-engine    |\n    +--------------+  +---------------+  +---------------+\n            \\           /       \\              /\n             \\         /         \\            /\n              \\       /           \\          /\n              +----- Event Bus (NATS / Kafka) -+\n                        ^\n                        |\n                 +---------------+\n                 |  AuditTrail   |\n                 +---------------+\n```\n\n## Event Catalog (Ubiquitous Language)\n\n* `StudentRegistered`\n* `InvoiceRaised`\n* `PaymentAuthorized`\n* `AidDisbursed`\n* `LedgerEntryPosted`\n* `SagaCompensationRequired`\n\n### Example Domain Event (C, Protobuf-ish Header)\n\n```c\n/* events/payment_authorized.h */\n#ifndef EP_EVENTS_PAYMENT_AUTH_H\n#define EP_EVENTS_PAYMENT_AUTH_H\n/*\n  Domain Event: PaymentAuthorized\n  This event is emitted by ledger-core after the acquiring bank\n  responds with an authorization code.  Other contexts (Financial-Aid,\n  Continuing-Education) subscribe to project read models.\n*/\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n#define PAYMENT_AUTH_VERSION 1\n\ntypedef struct ep_payment_auth_t {\n    uint8_t  version;          /* schema version                     */\n    char     id[37];           /* UUID v4 string                     */\n    char     student_id[16];   /* canonical SID                      */\n    char     invoice_id[37];   /* payment belongs to which invoice   */\n    char     currency[4];      /* ISO-4217                           */\n    int64_t  amount_minor;     /* 1099 = $10.99 ( if cents )         */\n    char     auth_code[12];    /* provided by payment processor      */\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;  /* RFC 3339 ts                        */\n} ep_payment_auth_t;\n\n#endif /* EP_EVENTS_PAYMENT_AUTH_H */\n```\n\n## Service Skeleton: `ledger-core`\n\nThe canonical micro-service exposes gRPC, publishes events on NATS,\nand persists to PostgreSQL.  Internally, Clean Architecture layers are\nsegregated into `domain`, `usecase`, and `infra` directories.\n\n### `domain/money.h`\n\n```c\n/* domain/money.h */\n#ifndef EP_DOMAIN_MONEY_H\n#define EP_DOMAIN_MONEY_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n\ntypedef struct ep_money_t {\n    int64_t amount_minor;  /* -922337203685477 */\n    char    currency[4];   /* \"USD\"            */\n} ep_money_t;\n\n/* Equality check without floating-point errors */\nstatic inline int ep_money_eq(const ep_money_t *a, const ep_money_t *b)\n{\n    return a && b &&\n           a->amount_minor == b->amount_minor &&\n           a->currency[0] == b->currency[0] &&\n           a->currency[1] == b->currency[1] &&\n           a->currency[2] == b->currency[2] &&\n           a->currency[3] == b->currency[3];\n}\n\n#endif /* EP_DOMAIN_MONEY_H */\n```\n\n### `usecase/post_payment.c`\n\n```c\n/* usecase/post_payment.c */\n#include \"domain/money.h\"\n#include \"events/payment_authorized.h\"\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <string.h>\n\ntypedef struct ep_payment_repo ep_payment_repo_t;\ntypedef struct ep_event_bus   ep_event_bus_t;\n\n/* Dependency inversion via pure C interfaces */\nstruct ep_payment_repo {\n    int (*begin_tx)(ep_payment_repo_t *);\n    int (*commit_tx)(ep_payment_repo_t *);\n    int (*rollback_tx)(ep_payment_repo_t *);\n    int (*insert_ledger_entry)(ep_payment_repo_t *,\n                               const char  *invoice_id,\n                               const ep_money_t *amount,\n                               const char  *auth_code);\n};\n\nstruct ep_event_bus {\n    int (*publish)(ep_event_bus_t *, const void *evt, size_t sz);\n};\n\n/*\n  Post a payment to the double-entry ledger.\n\n  Returns 0 on success, < 0 on domain error, > 0 on infra error.\n*/\nint ep_uc_post_payment(ep_payment_repo_t *repo,\n                       ep_event_bus_t    *bus,\n                       const char        *invoice_id,\n                       const ep_money_t  *amount,\n                       const char        *auth_code)\n{\n    if (!repo || !bus || !invoice_id || !amount || !auth_code)\n        return -1; /* pre-condition failed */\n\n    if (repo->begin_tx(repo) != 0)\n        return  1; /* infra error */\n\n    if (repo->insert_ledger_entry(repo, invoice_id, amount, auth_code) != 0) {\n        repo->rollback_tx(repo);\n        return  2;\n    }\n\n    ep_payment_auth_t evt = {\n        .version        = PAYMENT_AUTH_VERSION,\n        .occurred_at_utc= time(NULL),\n    };\n    /* (Safe) string copy utilities omitted for brevity */\n    strncpy(evt.id,        \"UUID-GEN-STUB\", sizeof evt.id);\n    strncpy(evt.student_id,\"SID-LOOKUP-X\", sizeof evt.student_id);\n    strncpy(evt.invoice_id,invoice_id,     sizeof evt.invoice_id);\n    strncpy(evt.currency,  amount->currency, sizeof evt.currency);\n    evt.amount_minor = amount->amount_minor;\n    strncpy(evt.auth_code, auth_code, sizeof evt.auth_code);\n\n    if (bus->publish(bus, &evt, sizeof evt) != 0) {\n        repo->rollback_tx(repo);\n        return  3;\n    }\n\n    return repo->commit_tx(repo);\n}\n```\n\n### Saga Orchestrator (Distributed Tuition Payment)\n\n```c\n/* saga/tuition_payment_saga.h */\n#ifndef EP_SAGA_TUITION_PAYMENT_H\n#define EP_SAGA_TUITION_PAYMENT_H\n\n/*\n  TuitionPaymentSaga orchestrates:\n\n  1. Reserve Financial-Aid budget\n  2. Authorize card payment (Bursar)\n  3. Disburse stipends\n  4. Issue micro-credential revenue split\n\n  Compensation order is reverse.\n\n  State machine is stored in the EventStore; students step through\n  failures during outage simulations.\n*/\n\ntypedef enum {\n    SAGA_STEP_NONE = 0,\n    SAGA_STEP_AID_RESERVED,\n    SAGA_STEP_PAYMENT_AUTHORIZED,\n    SAGA_STEP_STIPEND_PAID,\n    SAGA_STEP_MICROCRED_SPLIT,\n    SAGA_STEP_DONE,\n    SAGA_STEP_FAILED\n} ep_saga_state_t;\n\n#endif /* EP_SAGA_TUITION_PAYMENT_H */\n```\n\n## Anti-corruption Layer (ACL) Sample\n\nAdmissions uses an external vendor for SIS and must translate its JSON\nschema into *StudentRegistered* events.\n\n```c\n/* acl/sis_adapter.c */\n#include <jansson.h>\n#include \"events/student_registered.h\"\n\n/* Returns 0 on success */\nint ep_acl_translate_sis_event(const char *json,\n                               ep_student_reg_t *out_evt)\n{\n    json_error_t err;\n    json_t *root = json_loads(json, 0, &err);\n    if (!root) return -1;\n\n    const char *sid   = json_string_value(json_object_get(root, \"sid\"));\n    const char *email = json_string_value(json_object_get(root, \"email\"));\n    if (!sid || !email) {\n        json_decref(root);\n        return -2;\n    }\n\n    strncpy(out_evt->student_id, sid, sizeof out_evt->student_id);\n    strncpy(out_evt->email,      email, sizeof out_evt->email);\n    out_evt->occurred_at_utc = time(NULL);\n\n    json_decref(root);\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\n## Data Ownership & ACID Boundaries\n\n* **Admissions** owns `Student` aggregate; others reference via SID.\n* **Ledger-core** owns `Invoice`, `LedgerEntry`.\n* **Financial-Aid** owns `Award`, `AidDisbursement`.\n* Shared Kernel\u2019s `AuditTrail` is append-only; no service can mutate.\n\n| Service        | DB Schema          | Tx Boundary (Local ACID)    |\n|----------------|--------------------|-----------------------------|\n| admissions     | `admissions.*`     | `Student`, `Applicant`      |\n| ledger-core    | `ledger.*`         | `Invoice`, `LedgerEntry`    |\n| aid-engine     | `aid.*`            | `Award`, `Disbursement`     |\n| micro-cred     | `microcred.*`      | `CourseRun`, `SplitPayout`  |\n\n## Resilience Policy\n\n1. Idempotent command handlers.\n2. At-least-once event delivery (NATS JetStream).\n3. Circuit-breaker around external PSP, open after 3 failures / 30 s.\n4. Saga compensation for inter-context failure.\n\n```c\n/* infra/circuit_breaker.h */\n#ifndef EP_INFRA_CIRCUIT_BREAKER_H\n#define EP_INFRA_CIRCUIT_BREAKER_H\n#include <time.h>\ntypedef enum { CB_CLOSED, CB_OPEN, CB_HALF_OPEN } cb_state_t;\n\ntypedef struct circuit_breaker {\n    cb_state_t state;\n    unsigned   failure_count;\n    time_t     last_failure;\n    unsigned   open_timeout_sec;\n    unsigned   threshold;\n} circuit_breaker_t;\n\nvoid cb_init(circuit_breaker_t *cb,\n             unsigned threshold,\n             unsigned open_timeout_sec);\n\nint  cb_before_request(circuit_breaker_t *cb);\nvoid cb_after_success(circuit_breaker_t *cb);\nvoid cb_after_failure(circuit_breaker_t *cb);\n\n#endif /* EP_INFRA_CIRCUIT_BREAKER_H */\n```\n\n## Build & Deployment Standards\n\n* `Dockerfile` uses scratch + `musl-clang` static linking \u21d2 6 MB images.\n* Each service exports `/livez` and `/readyz` over HTTP on port 8080.\n* Kubernetes Helm charts pin CPU/memory, configure HPA on NATS lag.\n\n---\n\n> \u201cArchitecture is about the important stuff\u2014whatever that is.\u201d  \n> \u2014 Ralph Johnson\n\nLearners should fork this repository, enable **Saga Pattern\nDemonstration Mode** (`make chaos-on`), and trigger the `tuition\ncheckout` flow.  When the intentional fault in step 2 forces a\nrollback, open the **AuditTrail dashboard** and correlate the saga\ncompensating transactions.\n\nHappy hacking!",

Domain Vocabulary  \n2. High Level Flow Diagram  \n3. Command Pipeline (Write Model)  \n4. Event Store Implementation (C)  \n5. Query Model & Projections  \n6. Consistency, Concurrency, and Idempotency  \n7. Failure Injection Labs  \n8. Further Reading\n\n---\n\n## 1. Domain Vocabulary\n\nTerm | Definition\n---- | ----------\n**Command** | An intent _to do_ something. Must either succeed or return an error.\n**Event** | A fact _that something happened_. Can never change or be removed.\n**Aggregate** | A transactional consistency boundary, e.g., `LedgerAccount`.\n**Projection / Read Model** | A denormalized view optimized for reads: dashboards, ledgers, etc.\n\n---\n\n## 2. High Level Flow Diagram\n\n```mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    actor Student\n    participant CMD as Command API\n    participant CH as Command Handler\n    participant ES as Event Store (append-only)\n    participant PR as Projector\n    participant RM as Read Model (SQLite)\n    Student->>CMD: POST /accounts/deposit\n    CMD->>CH: DepositFundsCommand\n    CH->>ES: Append(EventDeposited)\n    ES->>PR: Emit(EventDeposited)\n    PR->>RM: UPDATE balances\n    Student->>RM: GET /dashboard\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Command Pipeline (Write Model)\n\nBelow is a **compile-ready** excerpt (C17) showing how a `CommandBus` validates and dispatches commands to their handlers.  \nIt purposefully decouples IO so professors can mock the bus during unit tests.\n\n```c\n/* File: src/cqrs/command_bus.h */\n#ifndef EDU_PAY_COMMAND_BUS_H\n#define EDU_PAY_COMMAND_BUS_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stddef.h>\n#include \"utils/uuid.h\"\n\n/* ---------- Generic Command Definition ---------- */\ntypedef struct {\n    uuid_t   id;         /* Correlation ID for tracing */\n    uint64_t timestamp;  /* epoch millis (monotonic)   */\n    const char *type;    /* \"DepositFundsCommand\" etc  */\n    void     *payload;   /* domain-specific struct ptr */\n} command_t;\n\n/* Error codes follow POSIX semantics for reuse in shell scripts */\ntypedef enum {\n    CMD_OK          = 0,\n    CMD_ERR_INPUT   = 22,  /* EINVAL */\n    CMD_ERR_HANDLER = 38,  /* ENOSYS */\n    CMD_ERR_REJECT  = 35   /* EDEADLK \u2013 business rule violated */\n} command_status_e;\n\n/* Opaque route handle resolves to specific handler at runtime */\ntypedef command_status_e (*command_handler_f)(const command_t *cmd);\n\n/* Register handler */\nint command_bus_register(const char *type, command_handler_f fn);\n\n/* Dispatch (synchronous) */\ncommand_status_e command_bus_execute(const command_t *cmd);\n\n#endif /* EDU_PAY_COMMAND_BUS_H */\n```\n\n```c\n/* File: src/cqrs/command_bus.c */\n#include \"cqrs/command_bus.h\"\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include \"utils/hashtable.h\"\n\n/* --- Very light associative table (string \u2192 function ptr) --- */\nstatic hash_table_t *router = NULL;\n\nint command_bus_register(const char *type, command_handler_f fn) {\n    if (!type || !fn) return -CMD_ERR_INPUT;\n    if (!router) router = ht_create(32);\n    return ht_put(router, type, fn);\n}\n\ncommand_status_e command_bus_execute(const command_t *cmd) {\n    if (!cmd || !cmd->type) return CMD_ERR_INPUT;\n    command_handler_f fn = ht_get(router, cmd->type);\n    if (!fn) return CMD_ERR_HANDLER;\n    return fn(cmd);\n}\n```\n\nExample Domain Command + Handler:\n\n```c\n/* File: src/payments/commands/deposit_funds.h */\n#ifndef EDU_PAY_COMMAND_DEPOSIT_H\n#define EDU_PAY_COMMAND_DEPOSIT_H\n#include <stdint.h>\n\ntypedef struct {\n    char     account_id[36];\n    uint64_t amount_cents;\n    char     currency[4];        /* \"USD\" | \"EUR\" | etc. */\n} deposit_funds_payload_t;\n\n#endif\n```\n\n```c\n/* File: src/payments/handlers/deposit_funds_handler.c */\n#include \"cqrs/command_bus.h\"\n#include \"events/event_bus.h\"\n#include \"payments/commands/deposit_funds.h\"\n#include \"payments/events/funds_deposited.h\"\n#include \"domain/accounts_repository.h\"\n#include \"utils/clock.h\"\n#include \"utils/currency.h\"\n\nstatic command_status_e handle_deposit(const command_t *cmd)\n{\n    if (!cmd || !cmd->payload) return CMD_ERR_INPUT;\n    const deposit_funds_payload_t *pl = cmd->payload;\n\n    /* --- Business Rule Enforcement --- */\n    if (!currency_is_supported(pl->currency) || pl->amount_cents == 0)\n        return CMD_ERR_REJECT;\n\n    /* Optimistic lock fetch */\n    ledger_account_t acct;\n    if (accounts_repo_load(pl->account_id, &acct) != 0)\n        return CMD_ERR_REJECT; /* Unknown account */\n\n    /* Domain invariants can run here (e.g., AML limits) */\n    /* ... */\n\n    /* --- Produce Event (immutably) --- */\n    funds_deposited_event_t ev = {\n        .base.id        = uuid_v4(),\n        .base.timestamp = clock_epoch_ms(),\n        .base.type      = \"FundsDepositedEvent\",\n        .account_id     = {0},\n        .amount_cents   = pl->amount_cents,\n        .currency       = {0}\n    };\n    strncpy(ev.account_id, pl->account_id, sizeof(ev.account_id)-1);\n    strncpy(ev.currency, pl->currency,   sizeof(ev.currency)-1);\n\n    /* Persist via Event Bus (which writes through to Event Store) */\n    if (event_bus_publish((event_t *)&ev) != EVT_OK)\n        return CMD_ERR_HANDLER;\n\n    return CMD_OK;\n}\n\n/* Auto-register at startup */\n__attribute__((constructor))\nstatic void _deposit_register(void) {\n    command_bus_register(\"DepositFundsCommand\", handle_deposit);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Event Store Implementation (C)\n\nThe **Event Store** is append-only, leverages `mmap(2)` for re-play speed, and stores each record as length-prefixed JSON so that students can grep logs with *jq*.\n\n```c\n/* File: src/event_store/event_store.h */\n#ifndef EDU_PAY_EVENT_STORE_H\n#define EDU_PAY_EVENT_STORE_H\n\n#include <stddef.h>\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include \"events/event.h\"\n\n#define EVT_STORE_OK          0\n#define EVT_STORE_ERR_IO    (-5)\n#define EVT_STORE_ERR_FULL (-28)    /* ENOSPC */\n\n/* Append single event (thread-safe, fsync\u2019ed) */\nint event_store_append(const event_t *ev);\n\n/* Stream all events for replay (blocking). \n   Calls `callback` for each event; stop when it returns non-zero. */\ntypedef int (*event_stream_cb)(const event_t *ev, void *ctx);\nint event_store_stream(event_stream_cb callback, void *ctx);\n\n#endif\n```\n\n```c\n/* File: src/event_store/event_store.c */\n#define _POSIX_C_SOURCE 200809L\n#include \"event_store/event_store.h\"\n#include <fcntl.h>\n#include <sys/mman.h>\n#include <sys/stat.h>\n#include <unistd.h>\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include \"utils/serialize_json.h\"\n#include \"utils/spinlock.h\"\n\n#define EVENT_STORE_FILE \"./var/event_store.log\"\n#define MAX_EVENT_SIZE   4096   /* hard cap to aid undergrad sanity */\n\nstatic int fd = -1;\nstatic pthread_spinlock_t lock;\n\n__attribute__((constructor))\nstatic void _init_store(void) {\n    fd = open(EVENT_STORE_FILE, O_RDWR | O_CREAT | O_APPEND, 0640);\n    pthread_spin_init(&lock, PTHREAD_PROCESS_PRIVATE);\n}\n\n__attribute__((destructor))\nstatic void _close_store(void) {\n    if (fd != -1) close(fd);\n    pthread_spin_destroy(&lock);\n}\n\nint event_store_append(const event_t *ev)\n{\n    if (!ev) return EVT_STORE_ERR_IO;\n\n    char buffer[MAX_EVENT_SIZE];\n    ssize_t len = json_serialize_event(ev, buffer, sizeof(buffer));\n    if (len < 0) return EVT_STORE_ERR_IO;\n\n    /* Length-prefixed frame */\n    uint32_t nlen = (uint32_t)len;\n    pthread_spin_lock(&lock);\n    ssize_t w = write(fd, &nlen, sizeof(nlen));\n    w += write(fd, buffer, len);\n    fsync(fd);\n    pthread_spin_unlock(&lock);\n\n    return (w == (ssize_t)(sizeof(nlen) + len)) ? EVT_STORE_OK\n                                                : EVT_STORE_ERR_IO;\n}\n\nint event_store_stream(event_stream_cb cb, void *ctx)\n{\n    if (!cb) return EVT_STORE_ERR_IO;\n\n    int sfd = open(EVENT_STORE_FILE, O_RDONLY);\n    if (sfd < 0) return EVT_STORE_ERR_IO;\n\n    uint32_t nlen;\n    while (read(sfd, &nlen, sizeof(nlen)) == sizeof(nlen)) {\n        if (nlen > MAX_EVENT_SIZE) { close(sfd); return EVT_STORE_ERR_IO; }\n        char buffer[MAX_EVENT_SIZE];\n        if (read(sfd, buffer, nlen) != (ssize_t)nlen) break;\n\n        event_t *ev = json_deserialize_event(buffer, nlen);\n        if (!ev) continue;\n        if (cb(ev, ctx) != 0) { free(ev); break; }\n        free(ev);\n    }\n    close(sfd);\n    return EVT_STORE_OK;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Query Model & Projections\n\nRead models are **eventually consistent**. Every event published above is fanned-out to one or more *Projectors* that transform it into query-optimized databases (SQLite, Redis, CSV for Excel labs).\n\n```c\n/* File: src/projections/balance_projection.c */\n#include \"events/event_bus.h\"\n#include \"payments/events/funds_deposited.h\"\n#include \"database/sqlite.h\"\n\nstatic int on_funds_deposited(const event_t *ev)\n{\n    const funds_deposited_event_t *e = (const funds_deposited_event_t *)ev;\n    return sqlite_exec(\n        \"INSERT INTO account_balance(account_id, currency, balance_cents) \"\n        \"VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3) \"\n        \"ON CONFLICT(account_id, currency) \"\n        \"DO UPDATE SET balance_cents = balance_cents + excluded.balance_cents;\",\n        e->account_id, e->currency, (int64_t)e->amount_cents);\n}\n\n__attribute__((constructor))\nstatic void _register_projector(void) {\n    event_bus_subscribe(\"FundsDepositedEvent\", on_funds_deposited);\n}\n```\n\nStudents can query via the REST shell or `sqlite3 var/read_models.db`.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Consistency, Concurrency, and Idempotency\n\n\u2022 **Concurrency Control** \u2013 Each aggregate carries a monotonically increasing `version`. Handlers pass the expected `version` into `event_store_append()`.  \n\u2022 **At-Least-Once Delivery** \u2013 Projectors keep an `offset` table so they can re-play events idempotently.  \n\u2022 **Snap-Shots** \u2013 Long-lived aggregates (>2 000 events) periodically persist snapshots to avoid hot-loop rehydration in class.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Failure Injection Labs\n\nActivate with:\n\n```bash\n# Simulate projector downtime\n$ make simulate_projector_outage DURATION=30s\n\n# Induce write-model crash mid-transaction\n$ make chaos_saga MODULE=payments\n```\n\nStudents then debug replay & compensating actions per the **Saga Pattern**.\n\n---\n\n## 8. inline rmq_status_t\n_rmq_parse_reply(amqp_rpc_reply_t reply)\n{\n    switch (reply.reply_type) {\n        case AMQP_RESPONSE_NORMAL:\n            return RMQ_OK;\n\n        case AMQP_RESPONSE_LIBRARY_EXCEPTION:\n            return (reply.library_error == AMQP_STATUS_CONNECTION_CLOSED)\n                   ? RMQ_ERROR_NOT_INITIALIZED\n                   : RMQ_ERROR_RPC;\n\n        case AMQP_RESPONSE_SERVER_EXCEPTION:\n            /* We treat all server exceptions the same here; caller\n             * will introspect diagnostic struct for details. */\n            return RMQ_ERROR_RPC;\n\n        default:\n            return RMQ_ERROR_RPC;\n    }\n}\n\n/* Populate diagnostic record */\nstatic inline void\n_rmq_set_diag(rmq_publisher_t *pub,\n              rmq_status_t     status,\n              const char      *ctx,\n              amqp_rpc_reply_t reply)\n{\n    if (!pub) { return; }\n\n    pub->last_diag.status    = status;\n    strncpy(pub->last_diag.context, ctx, sizeof(pub->last_diag.context)-1);\n    pub->last_diag.context[sizeof(pub->last_diag.context)-1] = '\\0';\n    pub->last_diag.timestamp = time(NULL);\n\n    if (reply.reply_type == AMQP_RESPONSE_SERVER_EXCEPTION) {\n        /* Convert server-exception to human-readable */\n        if (reply.reply.id == AMQP_CONNECTION_CLOSE_METHOD) {\n            amqp_connection_close_t *m = (amqp_connection_close_t *)reply.reply.decoded;\n            snprintf(pub->last_diag.broker_reply,\n                     sizeof(pub->last_diag.broker_reply),\n                     \"CONN_CLOSE: code=%u, text=%.*s\",\n                     m->reply_code,\n                     (int)m->reply_text.len,\n                     (char *)m->reply_text.bytes);\n        } else if (reply.reply.id == AMQP_CHANNEL_CLOSE_METHOD) {\n            amqp_channel_close_t *m = (amqp_channel_close_t *)reply.reply.decoded;\n            snprintf(pub->last_diag.broker_reply,\n                     sizeof(pub->last_diag.broker_reply),\n                     \"CHAN_CLOSE: code=%u, text=%.*s\",\n                     m->reply_code,\n                     (int)m->reply_text.len,\n                     (char *)m->reply_text.bytes);\n        } else {\n            snprintf(pub->last_diag.broker_reply,\n                     sizeof(pub->last_diag.broker_reply),\n                     \"SERVER_EXCEPTION id=%u\",\n                     reply.reply.id);\n        }\n    } else if (reply.reply_type == AMQP_RESPONSE_LIBRARY_EXCEPTION) {\n        snprintf(pub->last_diag.broker_reply,\n                 sizeof(pub->last_diag.broker_reply),\n                 \"LIB_EXCEPTION: %s\",\n                 amqp_error_string2(reply.library_error));\n    } else {\n        strncpy(pub->last_diag.broker_reply, \"OK\", sizeof(pub->last_diag.broker_reply)-1);\n    }\n}\n\n/* =========================================================================\n *  IMPLEMENTATION OF PUBLIC FUNCTIONS\n * ========================================================================= */\n\nstatic inline rmq_status_t\nrmq_publisher_init(rmq_publisher_t *pub,\n                   const char      *host,\n                   int              port,\n                   const char      *vhost,\n                   const char      *user,\n                   const char      *password,\n                   const char      *exchange,\n                   const char      *exchange_type,\n                   bool             declare,\n                   int              heartbeat)\n{\n    if (!pub) { return RMQ_ERROR_NOT_INITIALIZED; }\n\n    if (pub->is_open) {\n        _rmq_set_diag(pub, RMQ_ERROR_ALREADY_OPEN, \"init\", (amqp_rpc_reply_t){0});\n        return RMQ_ERROR_ALREADY_OPEN;\n    }\n\n    memset(pub, 0, sizeof(*pub));\n    pub->conn = amqp_new_connection();\n    pub->socket = amqp_tcp_socket_new(pub->conn);\n    if (!pub->socket) {\n        _rmq_set_diag(pub, RMQ_ERROR_SOCKET_CREATE, \"tcp_socket_new\", (amqp_rpc_reply_t){0});\n        return RMQ_ERROR_SOCKET_CREATE;\n    }\n\n    if (amqp_socket_open(pub->socket, host ? host : EDUPAY_RMQ_DEFAULT_HOST,\n                         port > 0 ? port : EDUPAY_RMQ_DEFAULT_PORT)) {\n        _rmq_set_diag(pub, RMQ_ERROR_SOCKET_OPEN, \"socket_open\", (amqp_rpc_reply_t){0});\n        return RMQ_ERROR_SOCKET_OPEN;\n    }\n\n    /* Login */\n    amqp_rpc_reply_t reply = amqp_login(pub->conn,\n                                        vhost ? vhost : EDUPAY_RMQ_DEFAULT_VHOST,\n                                        /* channel max */ 0,\n                                        /* frame max */    131072,\n                                        heartbeat > 0 ? heartbeat : EDUPAY_RMQ_DEFAULT_HEARTBEAT,\n                                        AMQP_SASL_METHOD_PLAIN,\n                                        user     ? user     : EDUPAY_RMQ_DEFAULT_USER,\n                                        password ? password : EDUPAY_RMQ_DEFAULT_PASSWORD);\n\n    rmq_status_t st = _rmq_parse_reply(reply);\n    if (st != RMQ_OK) {\n        _rmq_set_diag(pub, RMQ_ERROR_LOGIN, \"amqp_login\", reply);\n        return RMQ_ERROR_LOGIN;\n    }\n\n    /* Channel */\n    pub->channel_id = 1;\n    reply = amqp_channel_open(pub->conn, pub->channel_id);\n    st = _rmq_parse_reply(reply);\n    if (st != RMQ_OK) {\n        _rmq_set_diag(pub, RMQ_ERROR_CHANNEL_OPEN, \"channel_open\", reply);\n        return RMQ_ERROR_CHANNEL_OPEN;\n    }\n\n    strncpy(pub->exchange, exchange, sizeof(pub->exchange)-1);\n    pub->exchange[sizeof(pub->exchange)-1] = '\\0';\n\n    if (declare) {\n        amqp_exchange_declare(pub->conn, pub->channel_id,\n                              amqp_cstring_bytes(exchange),\n                              amqp_cstring_bytes(exchange_type ? exchange_type : \"topic\"),\n                              /* passive */ 0,\n                              /* durable */ 1,\n                              /* auto-delete */ 0,\n                              /* internal */ 0,\n                              amqp_empty_table);\n\n        reply = amqp_get_rpc_reply(pub->conn);\n        st = _rmq_parse_reply(reply);\n        if (st != RMQ_OK) {\n            _rmq_set_diag(pub, RMQ_ERROR_EXCHANGE_DECLARE, \"exchange_declare\", reply);\n            return RMQ_ERROR_EXCHANGE_DECLARE;\n        }\n        pub->exchange_declared = true;\n    }\n\n    pub->is_open = true;\n    _rmq_set_diag(pub, RMQ_OK, \"init\", reply);\n    return RMQ_OK;\n}\n\nstatic inline rmq_status_t\nrmq_publisher_publish_json(rmq_publisher_t *pub,\n                           const char      *routing_key,\n                           const char      *json_payload,\n                           bool             persistent)\n{\n    if (!pub || !pub->is_open) { return RMQ_ERROR_NOT_INITIALIZED; }\n    if (!json_payload)        { return RMQ_ERROR_PUBLISH; }\n\n    size_t len = strlen(json_payload);\n    return rmq_publisher_publish_bytes(pub,\n                                       routing_key,\n                                       (const uint8_t*)json_payload,\n                                       len,\n                                       \"application/json\",\n                                       persistent);\n}\n\nstatic inline rmq_status_t\nrmq_publisher_publish_bytes(rmq_publisher_t *pub,\n                            const char      *routing_key,\n                            const uint8_t   *payload,\n                            size_t           len,\n                            const char      *content_type,\n                            bool             persistent)\n{\n    if (!pub || !pub->is_open)           { return RMQ_ERROR_NOT_INITIALIZED; }\n    if (!payload || len == 0)            { return RMQ_ERROR_PUBLISH; }\n\n    amqp_basic_properties_t props;\n    props._flags = AMQP_BASIC_CONTENT_TYPE_FLAG\n                 | AMQP_BASIC_DELIVERY_MODE_FLAG\n                 | AMQP_BASIC_TIMESTAMP_FLAG;\n\n    props.content_type = amqp_cstring_bytes(content_type ? content_type : \"application/octet-stream\");\n    props.delivery_mode = persistent ? 2 : 1; /* 1 = non-persistent, 2 = persistent */\n    props.timestamp = (uint64_t)time(NULL);\n\n    int rc = amqp_basic_publish(pub->conn,\n                                pub->channel_id,\n                                amqp_cstring_bytes(pub->exchange),\n                                amqp_cstring_bytes(routing_key ? routing_key : \"\"),\n                                /* mandatory */ 0,\n                                /* immediate */ 0,\n                                &props,\n                                amqp_bytes_t{ .len = len, .bytes = (void*)payload });\n\n    if (rc != 0) {\n        _rmq_set_diag(pub, RMQ_ERROR_PUBLISH, \"basic_publish(io)\", (amqp_rpc_reply_t){0});\n        return RMQ_ERROR_PUBLISH;\n    }\n\n    /* For confirmation-mode, we would wait for Basic.Ack here. */\n    _rmq_set_diag(pub, RMQ_OK, \"publish\", (amqp_rpc_reply_t){0});\n    return RMQ_OK;\n}\n\nstatic inline void\nrmq_publisher_teardown(rmq_publisher_t *pub)\n{\n    if (!pub || !pub->is_open) { return; }\n\n    /* Close channel */\n    amqp_channel_close(pub->conn, pub->channel_id, AMQP_REPLY_SUCCESS);\n\n    /* Close connection */\n    amqp_connection_close(pub->conn, AMQP_REPLY_SUCCESS);\n    amqp_destroy_connection(pub->conn);\n\n    /* Reset */\n    memset(pub, 0, sizeof(*pub));\n}\n\nstatic inline const rmq_diagnostic_t*\nrmq_publisher_last_diag(const rmq_publisher_t *pub)\n{\n    return pub ? &pub->last_diag : NULL;\n}\n\n#endif /* EDU_PAY_RABBITMQ_PUBLISHER_HEADER_ONLY_GUARD */\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\n} /* extern \"C\" */\n#endif\n#endif /*   "content": "# Architectural Proposal: Tuition Auto-Payment Feature\n\n**Document Version:** 1.0\n**Date:** 2026-02-02\n**Author:** Senior Software Architect\n**Status:** Draft for Review\n\n---\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis document presents a detailed architectural proposal for implementing the new **Tuition Auto-Payment** feature in the EduPay Ledger Academy platform. The feature automatically applies a student's newly disbursed financial aid stipend towards their outstanding tuition balance, contingent upon explicit opt-in consent from the student.\n\nThe proposed design:\n- **Extends the existing `DisburseStipendSaga`** rather than creating a new saga\n- Maintains strict adherence to **Clean Architecture**, **CQRS/Event Sourcing**, and the **Saga Pattern**\n- Ensures **regulatory compliance** (FERPA, PCI-DSS) through consent-driven workflows\n- Preserves **eventual consistency** across bounded contexts\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Interaction Diagram/Sequence](#1-interaction-diagramsequence)\n2. [Saga Pattern Integration](#2-saga-pattern-integration)\n3. [New Domain Events](#3-new-domain-events)\n4. [CQRS/Event Sourcing Impact](#4-cqrsevent-sourcing-impact)\n5. [Compliance and Consent](#5-compliance-and-consent)\n6. [Affected Components](#6-affected-components)\n7. [Implementation Recommendations](#7-implementation-recommendations)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Interaction Diagram/Sequence\n\n### 1.1 High-Level Sequence Flow\n\nThe Tuition Auto-Payment feature introduces a new step in the stipend disbursement workflow that occurs **after** the stipend is successfully disbursed but **before** the saga completes. Below is the complete sequence:\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502  Financial Aid  \u2502    \u2502 DisburseStipendSaga     \u2502    \u2502   Projections Service   \u2502    \u2502  Bursar Service   \u2502    \u2502   Event Store     \u2502\n\u2502    Service      \u2502    \u2502   (Orchestrator)        \u2502    \u2502   (Read Model)          \u2502    \u2502  (ledger-core)    \u2502    \u2502  (Postgres/ES)    \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n         \u2502                          \u2502                             \u2502                           \u2502                         \u2502\n         \u2502 1.   \u2502\n```\n\n### 1.2 Detailed Step Breakdown\n\n| Step | Actor | Action | Description |\n|------|-------|--------|-------------|\n| 1-6 | DisburseStipendSaga | Existing Steps | Validate eligibility, reserve budget, initiate transfer, record ledger, publish `StipendDisbursed` |\n| 7a | Saga Coordinator | Query `GetAutoPaymentStatus` | Queries the projections_service read model for: (1) student's opt-in consent flag, (2) outstanding tuition balance |\n| 7b | Saga Coordinator | Command `ApplyStipendToTuition` | If opt-in=true AND balance>0, sends command to bursar_service |\n| 7c | Bursar Service | Process Command | Calculates application amount (min of stipend and balance), creates ledger entries |\n| 7d | Bursar Service | Publish Events | Emits `StipendAppliedToTuition` or `StipendApplicationToTuitionFailed` |\n| 8 | Saga Coordinator | Complete | Saga terminates successfully |\n\n### 1.3 Conditional Flow Logic\n\n```c\n// Pseudo-code for Step 7 decision logic\nif (query_auto_payment_status(student_id, &status) == QUERY_OK) {\n    if (status.opt_in_consent == true && status.tuition_balance_due > 0) {\n        int64_t apply_amount = MIN(stipend_amount, status.tuition_balance_due);\n        apply_stipend_to_tuition_command cmd = {\n            .student_id = student_id,\n            .stipend_disbursement_id = disbursement_id,\n            .amount_to_apply = apply_amount,\n            .currency = \"USD\"\n        };\n        bursar_service_execute(&cmd);\n    }\n    // If opt_in=false OR balance=0, skip auto-payment (no error)\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Saga Pattern Integration\n\n### 2.1 Design Decision: Extend Existing Saga\n\n**Recommendation:** Extend the existing `DisburseStipendSaga` in `/app/project/src/services/financial_aid_service/application/use_cases/disburse_stipend_saga.h` rather than creating a new saga.\n\n**Justification:**\n\n1. **Transactional Coherence**: Applying financial aid to tuition is a logical extension of the stipend disbursement process. The funds should be applied atomically as part of the same business transaction context.\n\n2. **Shared Correlation ID**: The existing saga's `correlation_id_t` can propagate through to the tuition application, maintaining a complete audit trail.\n\n3. **Unified Compensation**: If the tuition application step fails, compensation can leverage the existing rollback infrastructure (release_budget, reverse_transfer).\n\n4. **Simpler Mental Model**: A single saga for \"disburse stipend and optionally apply to tuition\" is easier to reason about than two separate sagas coordinating.\n\n5. **Existing Pattern Compatibility**: The current saga already follows the VTable callback pattern (see lines 147-155 of `disburse_stipend_saga.h`), making extension straightforward.\n\n### 2.2 Extended Saga Definition\n\n```c\n/* Extended callbacks for disburse_stipend_saga.h */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    bool     opt_in_consent;\n    int64_t  tuition_balance_due;\n    char     currency[4];\n} auto_payment_status_t;\n\n/* New callback: Query auto-payment eligibility */\ntypedef bool (*query_auto_payment_status_fn)(\n    uint64_t                   student_id,\n    auto_payment_status_t     *status_out,\n    saga_error_t              *err_out);\n\n/* New callback: Apply stipend to tuition */\ntypedef bool (*apply_stipend_to_tuition_fn)(\n    const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n    int64_t                               amount_to_apply,\n    uint64_t                             *ledger_entry_id_out,\n    saga_error_t                         *err_out);\n\n/* New callback: Reverse tuition application (compensation) */\ntypedef bool (*reverse_tuition_application_fn)(\n    uint64_t       ledger_entry_id,\n    saga_error_t  *err_out);\n\n/* Extended VTable */\ntypedef struct {\n    /* Existing callbacks */\n    validate_eligibility_fn   validate_eligibility;\n    reserve_budget_fn         reserve_budget;\n    release_budget_fn         release_budget;\n    initiate_transfer_fn      initiate_transfer;\n    reverse_transfer_fn       reverse_transfer;\n    record_ledger_entry_fn    record_ledger_entry;\n    publish_domain_event_fn   publish_domain_event;\n\n    /* NEW: Auto-payment callbacks */\n    query_auto_payment_status_fn   query_auto_payment_status;\n    apply_stipend_to_tuition_fn    apply_stipend_to_tuition;\n    reverse_tuition_application_fn reverse_tuition_application;\n} stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t;\n```\n\n### 2.3 Extended Saga Steps\n\nThe modified saga flow adds a new **Step 6** (inserted between existing steps 5 and the completion):\n\n| Step | Name | Forward Action | Compensation |\n|------|------|----------------|--------------|\n| 1 | Validate Eligibility | `validate_eligibility()` | N/A (no state change) |\n| 2 | Reserve Budget | `reserve_budget()` | `release_budget()` |\n| 3 | Initiate Transfer | `initiate_transfer()` | `reverse_transfer()` |\n| 4 | Record Ledger Entry | `record_ledger_entry()` | Ledger reversal entry |\n| 5 | Publish Domain Event | `publish_domain_event(\"StipendDisbursed\")` | Record reversal event |\n| **6** | **Apply to Tuition (Conditional)** | `apply_stipend_to_tuition()` | `reverse_tuition_application()` |\n\n### 2.4 Compensation Chain\n\nIf **Step 6 fails** after the tuition application was partially or fully processed:\n\n```c\n/* Compensation sequence for Step 6 failure */\nbool compensation_step_6(saga_context_t *ctx) {\n    saga_error_t err = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n\n    // Step 6 compensation: Reverse tuition application\n    if (ctx->tuition_ledger_entry_id != 0) {\n        cb->reverse_tuition_application(ctx->tuition_ledger_entry_id, &err);\n    }\n\n    // Continue with existing compensation chain (steps 5 -> 4 -> 3 -> 2)\n    cb->record_ledger_entry(req, \"STIPEND_DISBURSEMENT_REVERSED\", ctx->network_tx_id, &err);\n    cb->reverse_transfer(ctx->network_tx_id, &err);\n    cb->release_budget(ctx->reservation_id, &err);\n\n    return true; // Best-effort compensation\n}\n```\n\n### 2.5 Idempotency Considerations\n\nPer the saga documentation at `/app/project/docs/architecture/04_saga_pattern.md` (lines 382-386):\n\n> \"Compensations are **idempotent**: every reverse handler can run twice safely, a mandatory property in at-least-once delivery environments.\"\n\nThe `reverse_tuition_application_fn` must:\n1. Accept a `ledger_entry_id` for precise targeting\n2. Check if reversal already exists before creating\n3. Use the same `correlation_id` for traceability\n\n---\n\n## 3. New Domain Events\n\n### 3.1 Event Definitions\n\nThree new domain events are required:\n\n#### 3.1.1 `StipendAppliedToTuition`\n\n**Publisher:** `bursar_service`\n**Consumers:** `projections_service`, `notifications_service` (future), audit trail\n\n```c\n/* events/stipend_applied_to_tuition.h */\n#ifndef EDUPAY_EVENT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION_H\n#define EDUPAY_EVENT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n#define STIPEND_APPLIED_EVENT_VERSION 1\n\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];              /* UUID v4 */\n    char     correlation_id[37];        /* Links to original StipendDisbursed */\n\n    /* Student identification */\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    char     student_account_id[32];\n\n    /* Transaction details */\n    uint64_t stipend_disbursement_id;   /* FK to StipendDisbursed event */\n    uint64_t ledger_entry_id;           /* Bursar ledger entry */\n\n    /* Monetary details */\n    int64_t  amount_applied_minor;      /* Amount in minor units (cents) */\n    int64_t  remaining_stipend_minor;   /* Leftover stipend not applied */\n    int64_t  remaining_balance_minor;   /* Outstanding tuition after application */\n    char     currency[4];               /* ISO-4217 */\n\n    /* Timestamps */\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n    char     term[8];                   /* e.g., \"2024SP\" */\n} stipend_applied_to_tuition_event_t;\n\n#endif\n```\n\n#### 3.1.2 `StipendApplicationToTuitionFailed`\n\n**Publisher:** `bursar_service`\n**Consumers:** `projections_service`, `alerting_service`, audit trail\n\n```c\n/* events/stipend_application_failed.h */\n#ifndef EDUPAY_EVENT_STIPEND_APPLICATION_FAILED_H\n#define EDUPAY_EVENT_STIPEND_APPLICATION_FAILED_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\ntypedef enum {\n    APPLY_FAIL_ACCOUNT_SUSPENDED,\n    APPLY_FAIL_ACCOUNT_CLOSED,\n    APPLY_FAIL_CURRENCY_MISMATCH,\n    APPLY_FAIL_LEDGER_ERROR,\n    APPLY_FAIL_CONSENT_WITHDRAWN,\n    APPLY_FAIL_NO_BALANCE_DUE,\n    APPLY_FAIL_INTERNAL\n} stipend_application_failure_reason_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];\n    char     correlation_id[37];\n\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    uint64_t stipend_disbursement_id;\n\n    stipend_application_failure_reason_t reason;\n    char     error_message[128];\n\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n} stipend_application_failed_event_t;\n\n#endif\n```\n\n#### 3.1.3 `TuitionApplicationReversed`\n\n**Publisher:** `bursar_service` (during saga compensation)\n**Consumers:** `projections_service`, audit trail\n\n```c\n/* events/tuition_application_reversed.h */\n#ifndef EDUPAY_EVENT_TUITION_APPLICATION_REVERSED_H\n#define EDUPAY_EVENT_TUITION_APPLICATION_REVERSED_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];\n    char     correlation_id[37];\n\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    uint64_t original_ledger_entry_id;\n    uint64_t reversal_ledger_entry_id;\n\n    int64_t  amount_reversed_minor;\n    char     currency[4];\n\n    char     reason[128];              /* e.g., \"Saga compensation\" */\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n} tuition_application_reversed_event_t;\n\n#endif\n```\n\n### 3.2 Event Flow Diagram\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 CQRS/Event Sourcing Impact\n\n### 4.1 Write Model (Event Store) Changes\n\n#### 4.1.1 New Event Types in Event Store\n\nThe following new event types must be registered with the event store interface defined in `/app/project/src/core/event_sourcing/event_store_interface.h`:\n\n```c\n/* Add to event type registry */\nstatic const char* EVENT_TYPES[] = {\n    /* Existing */\n    \"PaymentAuthorized\",\n    \"StipendDisbursed\",\n    /* ... */\n\n    /* New for Auto-Payment */\n    \"StipendAppliedToTuition\",\n    \"StipendApplicationToTuitionFailed\",\n    \"TuitionApplicationReversed\"\n};\n```\n\n#### 4.1.2 Affected Aggregates in Bursar Service\n\n**1. Account Aggregate** (`/app/project/src/services/bursar_service/domain/account.h`):\n\nThe `account_credit` and `account_debit` functions (lines 155-187) will be invoked during the auto-payment process. No modifications needed to the aggregate itself, but new event handlers must be wired:\n\n```c\n/* In bursar_service command handler */\nAccountResult result = account_debit(\n    student_account,    /* Source: student's stipend funds */\n    amount_to_apply,\n    currency,\n    trace_id\n);\n\nif (result == ACC_OK) {\n    // Credit tuition receivables account\n    result = account_credit(\n        tuition_account,\n        amount_to_apply,\n        currency,\n        trace_id\n    );\n}\n```\n\n**2. Ledger Aggregate** (`/app/project/src/services/bursar_service/domain/ledger.h`):\n\nNew ledger entries must be created using `ledger_entry_create()` (lines 196-212):\n\n```c\n/* Create ledger entry for tuition payment */\nledger_entry_t entry;\nledger_entry_create(\n    &entry,\n    student_id,\n    \"TUITION_RECEIVABLE\",      /* account_id */\n    LEDGER_ENTRY_CREDIT,       /* type: credit reduces receivable */\n    amount,\n    \"Auto-payment from stipend disbursement\",\n    &correlation_id            /* links to saga */\n);\n\nledger_post_entry(ledger, &entry);\n```\n\n### 4.2 Read Model (Projections) Changes\n\n#### 4.2.1 Dashboard Projector Updates\n\nThe dashboard projector at `/app/project/src/projections_service/event_handlers/dashboard_projector.h` must be extended to handle the new events.\n\n**Current Event Types (lines 45-53):**\n```c\ntypedef enum {\n    EVT_UNDEFINED = 0,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_PROCESSED,\n    EVT_TRANSACTION_SETTLED,\n    EVT_FRAUD_FLAGGED,\n    EVT_CURRENCY_CONVERTED,\n    EVT_SCHOLARSHIP_DISBURSED\n} ledger_event_type_t;\n```\n\n**Extended Event Types:**\n```c\ntypedef enum {\n    EVT_UNDEFINED = 0,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_PROCESSED,\n    EVT_TRANSACTION_SETTLED,\n    EVT_FRAUD_FLAGGED,\n    EVT_CURRENCY_CONVERTED,\n    EVT_SCHOLARSHIP_DISBURSED,\n    /* NEW */\n    EVT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION,\n    EVT_STIPEND_APPLICATION_FAILED,\n    EVT_TUITION_APPLICATION_REVERSED\n} ledger_event_type_t;\n```\n\n**New Fold Function:**\n```c\n/* Add to dashboard_projector.h */\n\nstatic inline bool _fold_stipend_applied_to_tuition(sqlite3 *db,\n                                                     const char *payload)\n{\n    double amount = 0.0;\n    double remaining_balance = 0.0;\n\n    if (!_json_extract_double(payload, \"\\\"amount_applied_minor\\\"\", &amount))\n        return false;\n\n    _json_extract_double(payload, \"\\\"remaining_balance_minor\\\"\", &remaining_balance);\n\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    bool ok = false;\n\n    /* Update student's tuition dashboard */\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(\n            db,\n            \"UPDATE student_tuition_summary \"\n            \"SET tuition_paid = tuition_paid + ?, \"\n            \"    balance_due = ?, \"\n            \"    last_payment_date = datetime('now'), \"\n            \"    auto_payment_count = auto_payment_count + 1 \"\n            \"WHERE student_id = ?;\",\n            -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK)\n    {\n        sqlite3_bind_double(stmt, 1, amount / 100.0);  /* Convert cents to dollars */\n        sqlite3_bind_double(stmt, 2, remaining_balance / 100.0);\n        /* student_id binding would come from payload extraction */\n        ok = (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_DONE);\n    }\n\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return ok;\n}\n```\n\n**Update Event Handler Switch (around line 383):**\n```c\nswitch (evt->type) {\n    /* ... existing cases ... */\n\n    case EVT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION:\n        if (_json_extract_double(evt->payload, \"\\\"amount_applied_minor\\\"\", &amount))\n            fold_ok = _fold_stipend_applied_to_tuition(prj->db, evt->payload);\n        break;\n\n    case EVT_TUITION_APPLICATION_REVERSED:\n        /* Reverse the previous application */\n        if (_json_extract_double(evt->payload, \"\\\"amount_reversed_minor\\\"\", &amount))\n            fold_ok = _fold_tuition_application_reversed(prj->db, evt->payload);\n        break;\n\n    default:\n        fold_ok = true;\n        break;\n}\n```\n\n#### 4.2.2 New Read Model Tables\n\n```sql\n-- Auto-Payment Consent Tracking (for query in saga step 7a)\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS student_auto_payment_preferences (\n    student_id       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n    opt_in_consent   BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,\n    consent_date     DATETIME,\n    consent_version  INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,\n    updated_at       DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Student Tuition Summary (materialized view for dashboard)\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS student_tuition_summary (\n    student_id           TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n    tuition_charged      REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,\n    tuition_paid         REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,\n    balance_due          REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,\n    last_payment_date    DATETIME,\n    auto_payment_count   INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    updated_at           DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Auto-Payment History (for audit and student portal)\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS auto_payment_history (\n    id                      INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n    student_id              TEXT NOT NULL,\n    stipend_disbursement_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n    amount_applied          REAL NOT NULL,\n    remaining_stipend       REAL NOT NULL,\n    remaining_balance       REAL NOT NULL,\n    currency                TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'USD',\n    occurred_at             DATETIME NOT NULL,\n    created_at              DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n\n    FOREIGN KEY (student_id) REFERENCES student_auto_payment_preferences(student_id)\n);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Compliance and Consent\n\n### 5.1 Regulatory Framework\n\nAs documented in `/app/project/docs/architecture/05_security_and_compliance.md` and `/app/project/docs/lessons/L03_Regulatory_Compliance_in_Code.md`:\n\n| Regulation | Requirement | Implementation |\n|------------|-------------|----------------|\n| **FERPA** | Consent required for financial record access/modification | Explicit opt-in flag with versioned consent |\n| **PCI-DSS** | Secure handling of payment data | No PAN/CVV stored; use tokenized references |\n| **SOC 2** | Audit trail for all financial operations | Event sourcing provides immutable audit |\n\n### 5.2 Consent Storage and Management\n\n#### 5.2.1 Consent Data Model\n\nThe consent flag will be stored in a dedicated table maintained by the `admissions_service` (owner of Student aggregate) and projected to the read model:\n\n```c\n/* Domain: Student Preferences Aggregate (admissions_service) */\ntypedef struct {\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    bool     tuition_auto_pay_enabled;\n    time_t   consent_granted_at;\n    uint32_t consent_version;          /* For FERPA audit requirements */\n    char     consent_ip_address[46];   /* IPv6 max length */\n    char     consent_method[32];       /* \"web_portal\", \"mobile_app\", etc. */\n} student_auto_payment_consent_t;\n```\n\n#### 5.2.2 Consent Events\n\n```c\n/* Event: AutoPaymentConsentGranted */\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    bool     consent_granted;\n    uint32_t consent_version;\n    char     consent_method[32];\n    char     ip_address[46];\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n} auto_payment_consent_granted_event_t;\n\n/* Event: AutoPaymentConsentRevoked */\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    uint32_t previous_consent_version;\n    char     revocation_reason[128];\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n} auto_payment_consent_revoked_event_t;\n```\n\n### 5.3 Consent Check in Workflow\n\nThe consent check occurs in **Step 7a** of the extended saga:\n\n```c\n/* Implementation of query_auto_payment_status callback */\nbool impl_query_auto_payment_status(\n    uint64_t                student_id,\n    auto_payment_status_t  *status_out,\n    saga_error_t           *err_out)\n{\n    /* Query the read model (projections_service) */\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    bool found = false;\n\n    const char *sql =\n        \"SELECT p.opt_in_consent, t.balance_due, t.currency \"\n        \"FROM student_auto_payment_preferences p \"\n        \"LEFT JOIN student_tuition_summary t ON p.student_id = t.student_id \"\n        \"WHERE p.student_id = ?;\";\n\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(read_model_db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK) {\n        sqlite3_bind_int64(stmt, 1, (sqlite3_int64)student_id);\n\n        if (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_ROW) {\n            status_out->opt_in_consent = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 0) != 0;\n            status_out->tuition_balance_due = sqlite3_column_int64(stmt, 1);\n            strncpy(status_out->currency,\n                    (const char*)sqlite3_column_text(stmt, 2),\n                    sizeof(status_out->currency) - 1);\n            found = true;\n        }\n        sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    }\n\n    if (!found) {\n        /* No consent record = no opt-in (FERPA compliant default) */\n        status_out->opt_in_consent = false;\n        status_out->tuition_balance_due = 0;\n    }\n\n    return true;  /* Query succeeded (even if no data found) */\n}\n```\n\n### 5.4 FERPA Compliance Safeguards\n\nPer the compliance guard implementation in `/app/project/docs/lessons/L03_Regulatory_Compliance_in_Code.md`:\n\n1. **Explicit Consent Only**: Default is `opt_in_consent = false`\n2. **Consent Versioning**: Each consent update increments version number\n3. **Audit Trail**: All consent changes are event-sourced\n4. **Immediate Revocation**: Consent check happens at execution time, not at enrollment time\n5. **Description Scrubbing**: Use `ledger_ferpa_scrub()` (line 321 of `ledger.h`) on any student-identifiable information in ledger descriptions\n\n---\n\n## 6. Consent preferences table\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS student_auto_payment_preferences (\n    student_id       INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,\n    opt_in_consent   INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    consent_date     TEXT,\n    consent_version  INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,\n    updated_at       TEXT DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- 2. Auto-payment history for audit\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS auto_payment_history (\n    id                      INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n    student_id              INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    stipend_disbursement_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n    amount_applied          INTEGER NOT NULL,  -- minor units\n    remaining_stipend       INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    remaining_balance       INTEGER NOT NULL,\n    currency                TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'USD',\n    occurred_at             TEXT NOT NULL,\n    correlation_id          TEXT NOT NULL,\n    created_at              TEXT DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- 4. Index for student history queries\nCREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_auto_payment_history_student\nON auto_payment_history(student_id, occurred_at DESC);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Implementation Recommendations\n\n### 7.1 Phased Rollout\n\n**Phase 1: Infrastructure** (Week 1-2)\n- Create new event definitions\n- Add database migrations\n- Implement projector updates\n\n**Phase 2: Core Logic** (Week 3-4)\n- Extend `disburse_stipend_saga.h` with new callbacks\n- Implement `apply_stipend_to_tuition` use case in bursar_service\n- Wire command handlers\n\n**Phase 3: Rollout** (Week 6)\n- Feature flag controlled release\n- Monitor compensating action frequency\n- Gather metrics on auto-payment adoption\n\n### 7.2 Testing Strategy\n\n```c\n/* Test: Saga completes when consent is granted and balance exists */\nvoid test_auto_payment_happy_path(void) {\n    setup_student_with_consent(STUDENT_ID, true);\n    setup_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID, 500000);  // $5000.00\n\n    stipend_disbursement_request_t req = {\n        .student_id = STUDENT_ID,\n        .stipend_cents = 200000,  // $2000.00\n        .currency = \"USD\"\n    };\n\n    saga_error_t err;\n    bool result = disburse_stipend_run(&req, &test_callbacks, &err);\n\n    assert(result == true);\n    assert(err.code == SAGA_OK);\n    assert(get_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID) == 300000);  // $3000.00 remaining\n    assert(get_auto_payment_count(STUDENT_ID) == 1);\n}\n\n/* Test: Saga skips auto-payment when consent is not granted */\nvoid test_auto_payment_no_consent(void) {\n    setup_student_with_consent(STUDENT_ID, false);  // No consent\n    setup_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID, 500000);\n\n    stipend_disbursement_request_t req = { /* ... */ };\n\n    saga_error_t err;\n    bool result = disburse_stipend_run(&req, &test_callbacks, &err);\n\n    assert(result == true);  // Saga succeeds\n    assert(get_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID) == 500000);  // Unchanged\n    assert(get_auto_payment_count(STUDENT_ID) == 0);\n}\n\n/* Test: Compensation reverses auto-payment on later failure */\nvoid test_auto_payment_compensation(void) {\n    setup_student_with_consent(STUDENT_ID, true);\n    setup_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID, 500000);\n\n    test_callbacks.publish_domain_event = failing_publish;  // Inject failure\n\n    saga_error_t err;\n    bool result = disburse_stipend_run(&req, &test_callbacks, &err);\n\n    assert(result == false);\n    assert(err.code == SAGA_ERR_EVENT_BUS);\n    assert(get_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID) == 500000);  // Restored\n    assert(get_reversal_count(STUDENT_ID) == 1);  // Compensation ran\n}\n```\n\n### 7.3 Monitoring and Observability\n\nAdd OpenTelemetry spans (per production hardening checklist in `/app/project/docs/architecture/04_saga_pattern.md`):\n\n```c\n/* Tracing for auto-payment step */\nvoid trace_auto_payment_step(\n    const char *step_name,\n    uint64_t    student_id,\n    int64_t     amount,\n    bool        success)\n{\n    char trace_msg[256];\n    snprintf(trace_msg, sizeof(trace_msg),\n             \"[SAGA:AutoPayment] step=%s student=%\" PRIu64\n             \" amount=%\" PRId64 \" result=%s\",\n             step_name, student_id, amount,\n             success ? \"OK\" : \"FAILED\");\n\n    otel_span_add_event(current_span(), trace_msg);\n}\n```\n\n### 7.4 Feature Flag Configuration\n\n```c\n/* Runtime feature flag check */\nbool is_auto_payment_enabled(void) {\n    const char *flag = getenv(\"EDUPAY_AUTO_PAYMENT_ENABLED\");\n    return flag && *flag == '1';\n}\n\n/* In saga execution */\nif (is_auto_payment_enabled()) {\n    // Execute Step 6: Auto-payment\n    apply_stipend_to_tuition_if_eligible(req, cb, err_out);\n} else {\n    // Skip auto-payment (feature disabled)\n    log_info(\"Auto-payment feature disabled, skipping step 6\");\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## |\n|------|------------|\n| **Aggregate** | A cluster of domain objects treated as a single unit (DDD) |\n| **Bounded Context** | A logical boundary within which a particular model applies (DDD) |\n| **Compensation** | A rollback action that semantically undoes a forward saga step |\n| **CQRS** | Command Query Responsibility Segregation |\n| **Event Sourcing** | Storing state as a sequence of immutable events |\n| **Minor Units** | Currency amounts in smallest denomination (e.g., cents) |\n| **Projection** | A read-optimized view derived from event streams |\n| **Saga** | A sequence of local transactions with compensating actions |\n| **VTable** | A structure of function pointers for dependency injection |\n\n---\n\n*End of Architectural Proposal*\n",

{
  "content": "# Architectural Proposal: Tuition Auto-Payment Feature\n\n**Document Version:** 1.0\n**Date:** 2026-02-02\n**Author:** Senior Software Architect\n**Status:** Draft for Review\n\n---\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis document presents a detailed architectural proposal for implementing the new **Tuition Auto-Payment** feature in the EduPay Ledger Academy platform. The feature automatically applies a student's newly disbursed financial aid stipend towards their outstanding tuition balance, contingent upon explicit opt-in consent from the student.\n\nThe proposed design:\n- **Extends the existing `DisburseStipendSaga`** rather than creating a new saga\n- Maintains strict adherence to **Clean Architecture**, **CQRS/Event Sourcing**, and the **Saga Pattern**\n- Ensures **regulatory compliance** (FERPA, PCI-DSS) through consent-driven workflows\n- Preserves **eventual consistency** across bounded contexts\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Interaction Diagram/Sequence](#1-interaction-diagramsequence)\n2. [Saga Pattern Integration](#2-saga-pattern-integration)\n3. [New Domain Events](#3-new-domain-events)\n4. [CQRS/Event Sourcing Impact](#4-cqrsevent-sourcing-impact)\n5. [Compliance and Consent](#5-compliance-and-consent)\n6. [Affected Components](#6-affected-components)\n7. [Implementation Recommendations](#7-implementation-recommendations)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Interaction Diagram/Sequence\n\n### 1.1 High-Level Sequence Flow\n\nThe Tuition Auto-Payment feature introduces a new step in the stipend disbursement workflow that occurs **after** the stipend is successfully disbursed but **before** the saga completes. Below is the complete sequence:\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502  Financial Aid  \u2502    \u2502 DisburseStipendSaga     \u2502    \u2502   Projections Service   \u2502    \u2502  Bursar Service   \u2502    \u2502   Event Store     \u2502\n\u2502    Service      \u2502    \u2502   (Orchestrator)        \u2502    \u2502   (Read Model)          \u2502    \u2502  (ledger-core)    \u2502    \u2502  (Postgres/ES)    \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518    \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u252c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n         \u2502                          \u2502                             \u2502                           \u2502                         \u2502\n         \u2502 1.                         \u2502                         \u2502\n         \u2502                          \u2502                             \u2502                           \u2502                         \u2502\n```\n\n### 1.2 Detailed Step Breakdown\n\n| Step | Actor | Action | Description |\n|------|-------|--------|-------------|\n| 1-6 | DisburseStipendSaga | Existing Steps | Validate eligibility, reserve budget, initiate transfer, record ledger, publish `StipendDisbursed` |\n| 7a | Saga Coordinator | Query `GetAutoPaymentStatus` | Queries the projections_service read model for: (1) student's opt-in consent flag, (2) outstanding tuition balance |\n| 7b | Saga Coordinator | Command `ApplyStipendToTuition` | If opt-in=true AND balance>0, sends command to bursar_service |\n| 7c | Bursar Service | Process Command | Calculates application amount (min of stipend and balance), creates ledger entries |\n| 7d | Bursar Service | Publish Events | Emits `StipendAppliedToTuition` or `StipendApplicationToTuitionFailed` |\n| 8 | Saga Coordinator | Complete | Saga terminates successfully |\n\n### 1.3 Conditional Flow Logic\n\n```c\n// Pseudo-code for Step 7 decision logic\nif (query_auto_payment_status(student_id, &status) == QUERY_OK) {\n    if (status.opt_in_consent == true && status.tuition_balance_due > 0) {\n        int64_t apply_amount = MIN(stipend_amount, status.tuition_balance_due);\n        apply_stipend_to_tuition_command cmd = {\n            .student_id = student_id,\n            .stipend_disbursement_id = disbursement_id,\n            .amount_to_apply = apply_amount,\n            .currency = \"USD\"\n        };\n        bursar_service_execute(&cmd);\n    }\n    // If opt_in=false OR balance=0, skip auto-payment (no error)\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Saga Pattern Integration\n\n### 2.1 Design Decision: Extend Existing Saga\n\n**Recommendation:** Extend the existing `DisburseStipendSaga` in `/app/project/src/services/financial_aid_service/application/use_cases/disburse_stipend_saga.h` rather than creating a new saga.\n\n**Justification:**\n\n1. **Transactional Coherence**: Applying financial aid to tuition is a logical extension of the stipend disbursement process. The funds should be applied atomically as part of the same business transaction context.\n\n2. **Shared Correlation ID**: The existing saga's `correlation_id_t` can propagate through to the tuition application, maintaining a complete audit trail.\n\n3. **Unified Compensation**: If the tuition application step fails, compensation can leverage the existing rollback infrastructure (release_budget, reverse_transfer).\n\n4. **Simpler Mental Model**: A single saga for \"disburse stipend and optionally apply to tuition\" is easier to reason about than two separate sagas coordinating.\n\n5. **Existing Pattern Compatibility**: The current saga already follows the VTable callback pattern (see lines 147-155 of `disburse_stipend_saga.h`), making extension straightforward.\n\n### 2.2 Extended Saga Definition\n\n```c\n/* Extended callbacks for disburse_stipend_saga.h */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    bool     opt_in_consent;\n    int64_t  tuition_balance_due;\n    char     currency[4];\n} auto_payment_status_t;\n\n/* New callback: Query auto-payment eligibility */\ntypedef bool (*query_auto_payment_status_fn)(\n    uint64_t                   student_id,\n    auto_payment_status_t     *status_out,\n    saga_error_t              *err_out);\n\n/* New callback: Apply stipend to tuition */\ntypedef bool (*apply_stipend_to_tuition_fn)(\n    const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n    int64_t                               amount_to_apply,\n    uint64_t                             *ledger_entry_id_out,\n    saga_error_t                         *err_out);\n\n/* New callback: Reverse tuition application (compensation) */\ntypedef bool (*reverse_tuition_application_fn)(\n    uint64_t       ledger_entry_id,\n    saga_error_t  *err_out);\n\n/* Extended VTable */\ntypedef struct {\n    /* Existing callbacks */\n    validate_eligibility_fn   validate_eligibility;\n    reserve_budget_fn         reserve_budget;\n    release_budget_fn         release_budget;\n    initiate_transfer_fn      initiate_transfer;\n    reverse_transfer_fn       reverse_transfer;\n    record_ledger_entry_fn    record_ledger_entry;\n    publish_domain_event_fn   publish_domain_event;\n\n    /* NEW: Auto-payment callbacks */\n    query_auto_payment_status_fn   query_auto_payment_status;\n    apply_stipend_to_tuition_fn    apply_stipend_to_tuition;\n    reverse_tuition_application_fn reverse_tuition_application;\n} stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t;\n```\n\n### 2.3 Extended Saga Steps\n\nThe modified saga flow adds a new **Step 6** (inserted between existing steps 5 and the completion):\n\n| Step | Name | Forward Action | Compensation |\n|------|------|----------------|--------------|\n| 1 | Validate Eligibility | `validate_eligibility()` | N/A (no state change) |\n| 2 | Reserve Budget | `reserve_budget()` | `release_budget()` |\n| 3 | Initiate Transfer | `initiate_transfer()` | `reverse_transfer()` |\n| 4 | Record Ledger Entry | `record_ledger_entry()` | Ledger reversal entry |\n| 5 | Publish Domain Event | `publish_domain_event(\"StipendDisbursed\")` | Record reversal event |\n| **6** | **Apply to Tuition (Conditional)** | `apply_stipend_to_tuition()` | `reverse_tuition_application()` |\n\n### 2.4 Compensation Chain\n\nIf **Step 6 fails** after the tuition application was partially or fully processed:\n\n```c\n/* Compensation sequence for Step 6 failure */\nbool compensation_step_6(saga_context_t *ctx) {\n    saga_error_t err = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n\n    // Step 6 compensation: Reverse tuition application\n    if (ctx->tuition_ledger_entry_id != 0) {\n        cb->reverse_tuition_application(ctx->tuition_ledger_entry_id, &err);\n    }\n\n    // Continue with existing compensation chain (steps 5 -> 4 -> 3 -> 2)\n    cb->record_ledger_entry(req, \"STIPEND_DISBURSEMENT_REVERSED\", ctx->network_tx_id, &err);\n    cb->reverse_transfer(ctx->network_tx_id, &err);\n    cb->release_budget(ctx->reservation_id, &err);\n\n    return true; // Best-effort compensation\n}\n```\n\n### 2.5 Idempotency Considerations\n\nPer the saga documentation at `/app/project/docs/architecture/04_saga_pattern.md` (lines 382-386):\n\n> \"Compensations are **idempotent**: every reverse handler can run twice safely, a mandatory property in at-least-once delivery environments.\"\n\nThe `reverse_tuition_application_fn` must:\n1. Accept a `ledger_entry_id` for precise targeting\n2. Check if reversal already exists before creating\n3. Use the same `correlation_id` for traceability\n\n---\n\n## 3. New Domain Events\n\n### 3.1 Event Definitions\n\nThree new domain events are required:\n\n#### 3.1.1 `StipendAppliedToTuition`\n\n**Publisher:** `bursar_service`\n**Consumers:** `projections_service`, `notifications_service` (future), audit trail\n\n```c\n/* events/stipend_applied_to_tuition.h */\n#ifndef EDUPAY_EVENT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION_H\n#define EDUPAY_EVENT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n#define STIPEND_APPLIED_EVENT_VERSION 1\n\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];              /* UUID v4 */\n    char     correlation_id[37];        /* Links to original StipendDisbursed */\n\n    /* Student identification */\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    char     student_account_id[32];\n\n    /* Transaction details */\n    uint64_t stipend_disbursement_id;   /* FK to StipendDisbursed event */\n    uint64_t ledger_entry_id;           /* Bursar ledger entry */\n\n    /* Monetary details */\n    int64_t  amount_applied_minor;      /* Amount in minor units (cents) */\n    int64_t  remaining_stipend_minor;   /* Leftover stipend not applied */\n    int64_t  remaining_balance_minor;   /* Outstanding tuition after application */\n    char     currency[4];               /* ISO-4217 */\n\n    /* Timestamps */\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n    char     term[8];                   /* e.g., \"2024SP\" */\n} stipend_applied_to_tuition_event_t;\n\n#endif\n```\n\n#### 3.1.2 `StipendApplicationToTuitionFailed`\n\n**Publisher:** `bursar_service`\n**Consumers:** `projections_service`, `alerting_service`, audit trail\n\n```c\n/* events/stipend_application_failed.h */\n#ifndef EDUPAY_EVENT_STIPEND_APPLICATION_FAILED_H\n#define EDUPAY_EVENT_STIPEND_APPLICATION_FAILED_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\ntypedef enum {\n    APPLY_FAIL_ACCOUNT_SUSPENDED,\n    APPLY_FAIL_ACCOUNT_CLOSED,\n    APPLY_FAIL_CURRENCY_MISMATCH,\n    APPLY_FAIL_LEDGER_ERROR,\n    APPLY_FAIL_CONSENT_WITHDRAWN,\n    APPLY_FAIL_NO_BALANCE_DUE,\n    APPLY_FAIL_INTERNAL\n} stipend_application_failure_reason_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];\n    char     correlation_id[37];\n\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    uint64_t stipend_disbursement_id;\n\n    stipend_application_failure_reason_t reason;\n    char     error_message[128];\n\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n} stipend_application_failed_event_t;\n\n#endif\n```\n\n#### 3.1.3 `TuitionApplicationReversed`\n\n**Publisher:** `bursar_service` (during saga compensation)\n**Consumers:** `projections_service`, audit trail\n\n```c\n/* events/tuition_application_reversed.h */\n#ifndef EDUPAY_EVENT_TUITION_APPLICATION_REVERSED_H\n#define EDUPAY_EVENT_TUITION_APPLICATION_REVERSED_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];\n    char     correlation_id[37];\n\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    uint64_t original_ledger_entry_id;\n    uint64_t reversal_ledger_entry_id;\n\n    int64_t  amount_reversed_minor;\n    char     currency[4];\n\n    char     reason[128];              /* e.g., \"Saga compensation\" */\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n} tuition_application_reversed_event_t;\n\n#endif\n```\n\n### 3.2 Event Flow Diagram\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510
