CQRS/Event Sourcing Impact\n\n### 4.1 Write Model (Event Store) Changes\n\n#### 4.1.1 New Event Types in Event Store\n\nThe following new event types must be registered with the event store interface defined in `/app/project/src/core/event_sourcing/event_store_interface.h`:\n\n```c\n/* Add to event type registry */\nstatic const char* EVENT_TYPES[] = {\n    /* Existing */\n    \"PaymentAuthorized\",\n    \"StipendDisbursed\",\n    /* ... */\n\n    /* New for Auto-Payment */\n    \"StipendAppliedToTuition\",\n    \"StipendApplicationToTuitionFailed\",\n    \"TuitionApplicationReversed\"\n};\n```\n\n#### 4.1.2 Affected Aggregates in Bursar Service\n\n**1. Account Aggregate** (`/app/project/src/services/bursar_service/domain/account.h`):\n\nThe `account_credit` and `account_debit` functions (lines 155-187) will be invoked during the auto-payment process. No modifications needed to the aggregate itself, but new event handlers must be wired:\n\n```c\n/* In bursar_service command handler */\nAccountResult result = account_debit(\n    student_account,    /* Source: student's stipend funds */\n    amount_to_apply,\n    currency,\n    trace_id\n);\n\nif (result == ACC_OK) {\n    // Credit tuition receivables account\n    result = account_credit(\n        tuition_account,\n        amount_to_apply,\n        currency,\n        trace_id\n    );\n}\n```\n\n**2. Ledger Aggregate** (`/app/project/src/services/bursar_service/domain/ledger.h`):\n\nNew ledger entries must be created using `ledger_entry_create()` (lines 196-212):\n\n```c\n/* Create ledger entry for tuition payment */\nledger_entry_t entry;\nledger_entry_create(\n    &entry,\n    student_id,\n    \"TUITION_RECEIVABLE\",      /* account_id */\n    LEDGER_ENTRY_CREDIT,       /* type: credit reduces receivable */\n    amount,\n    \"Auto-payment from stipend disbursement\",\n    &correlation_id            /* links to saga */\n);\n\nledger_post_entry(ledger, &entry);\n```\n\n### 4.2 Read Model (Projections) Changes\n\n#### 4.2.1 Dashboard Projector Updates\n\nThe dashboard projector at `/app/project/src/projections_service/event_handlers/dashboard_projector.h` must be extended to handle the new events.\n\n**Current Event Types (lines 45-53):**\n```c\ntypedef enum {\n    EVT_UNDEFINED = 0,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_PROCESSED,\n    EVT_TRANSACTION_SETTLED,\n    EVT_FRAUD_FLAGGED,\n    EVT_CURRENCY_CONVERTED,\n    EVT_SCHOLARSHIP_DISBURSED\n} ledger_event_type_t;\n```\n\n**Extended Event Types:**\n```c\ntypedef enum {\n    EVT_UNDEFINED = 0,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_PROCESSED,\n    EVT_TRANSACTION_SETTLED,\n    EVT_FRAUD_FLAGGED,\n    EVT_CURRENCY_CONVERTED,\n    EVT_SCHOLARSHIP_DISBURSED,\n    /* NEW */\n    EVT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION,\n    EVT_STIPEND_APPLICATION_FAILED,\n    EVT_TUITION_APPLICATION_REVERSED\n} ledger_event_type_t;\n```\n\n**New Fold Function:**\n```c\n/* Add to dashboard_projector.h */\n\nstatic inline bool _fold_stipend_applied_to_tuition(sqlite3 *db,\n                                                     const char *payload)\n{\n    double amount = 0.0;\n    double remaining_balance = 0.0;\n\n    if (!_json_extract_double(payload, \"\\\"amount_applied_minor\\\"\", &amount))\n        return false;\n\n    _json_extract_double(payload, \"\\\"remaining_balance_minor\\\"\", &remaining_balance);\n\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    bool ok = false;\n\n    /* Update student's tuition dashboard */\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(\n            db,\n            \"UPDATE student_tuition_summary \"\n            \"SET tuition_paid = tuition_paid + ?, \"\n            \"    balance_due = ?, \"\n            \"    last_payment_date = datetime('now'), \"\n            \"    auto_payment_count = auto_payment_count + 1 \"\n            \"WHERE student_id = ?;\",\n            -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK)\n    {\n        sqlite3_bind_double(stmt, 1, amount / 100.0);  /* Convert cents to dollars */\n        sqlite3_bind_double(stmt, 2, remaining_balance / 100.0);\n        /* student_id binding would come from payload extraction */\n        ok = (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_DONE);\n    }\n\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return ok;\n}\n```\n\n**Update Event Handler Switch (around line 383):**\n```c\nswitch (evt->type) {\n    /* ... existing cases ... */\n\n    case EVT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION:\n        if (_json_extract_double(evt->payload, \"\\\"amount_applied_minor\\\"\", &amount))\n            fold_ok = _fold_stipend_applied_to_tuition(prj->db, evt->payload);\n        break;\n\n    case EVT_TUITION_APPLICATION_REVERSED:\n        /* Reverse the previous application */\n        if (_json_extract_double(evt->payload, \"\\\"amount_reversed_minor\\\"\", &amount))\n            fold_ok = _fold_tuition_application_reversed(prj->db, evt->payload);\n        break;\n\n    default:\n        fold_ok = true;\n        break;\n}\n```\n\n#### 4.2.2 New Read Model Tables\n\n```sql\n-- Auto-Payment Consent Tracking (for query in saga step 7a)\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS student_auto_payment_preferences (\n    student_id       TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n    opt_in_consent   BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,\n    consent_date     DATETIME,\n    consent_version  INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,\n    updated_at       DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Student Tuition Summary (materialized view for dashboard)\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS student_tuition_summary (\n    student_id           TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n    tuition_charged      REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,\n    tuition_paid         REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,\n    balance_due          REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,\n    last_payment_date    DATETIME,\n    auto_payment_count   INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,\n    updated_at           DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP\n);\n\n-- Auto-Payment History (for audit and student portal)\nCREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS auto_payment_history (\n    id                      INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n    student_id              TEXT NOT NULL,\n    stipend_disbursement_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n    amount_applied          REAL NOT NULL,\n    remaining_stipend       REAL NOT NULL,\n    remaining_balance       REAL NOT NULL,\n    currency                TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'USD',\n    occurred_at             DATETIME NOT NULL,\n    created_at              DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,\n\n    FOREIGN KEY (student_id) REFERENCES student_auto_payment_preferences(student_id)\n);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Compliance and Consent\n\n### 5.1 Regulatory Framework\n\nAs documented in `/app/project/docs/architecture/05_security_and_compliance.md` and `/app/project/docs/lessons/L03_Regulatory_Compliance_in_Code.md`:\n\n| Regulation | Requirement | Implementation |\n|------------|-------------|----------------|\n| **FERPA** | Consent required for financial record access/modification | Explicit opt-in flag with versioned consent |\n| **PCI-DSS** | Secure handling of payment data | No PAN/CVV stored; use tokenized references |\n| **SOC 2** | Audit trail for all financial operations | Event sourcing provides immutable audit |\n\n### 5.2 Consent Storage and Management\n\n#### 5.2.1 Consent Data Model\n\nThe consent flag will be stored in a dedicated table maintained by the `admissions_service` (owner of Student aggregate) and projected to the read model:\n\n```c\n/* Domain: Student Preferences Aggregate (admissions_service) */\ntypedef struct {\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    bool     tuition_auto_pay_enabled;\n    time_t   consent_granted_at;\n    uint32_t consent_version;          /* For FERPA audit requirements */\n    char     consent_ip_address[46];   /* IPv6 max length */\n    char     consent_method[32];       /* \"web_portal\", \"mobile_app\", etc. */\n} student_auto_payment_consent_t;\n```\n\n#### 5.2.2 Consent Events\n\n```c\n/* Event: AutoPaymentConsentGranted */\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    bool     consent_granted;\n    uint32_t consent_version;\n    char     consent_method[32];\n    char     ip_address[46];\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n} auto_payment_consent_granted_event_t;\n\n/* Event: AutoPaymentConsentRevoked */\ntypedef struct {\n    uint8_t  version;\n    char     event_id[37];\n    uint64_t student_id;\n    uint32_t previous_consent_version;\n    char     revocation_reason[128];\n    time_t   occurred_at_utc;\n} auto_payment_consent_revoked_event_t;\n```\n\n### 5.3 Consent Check in Workflow\n\nThe consent check occurs in **Step 7a** of the extended saga:\n\n```c\n/* Implementation of query_auto_payment_status callback */\nbool impl_query_auto_payment_status(\n    uint64_t                student_id,\n    auto_payment_status_t  *status_out,\n    saga_error_t           *err_out)\n{\n    /* Query the read model (projections_service) */\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    bool found = false;\n\n    const char *sql =\n        \"SELECT p.opt_in_consent, t.balance_due, t.currency \"\n        \"FROM student_auto_payment_preferences p \"\n        \"LEFT JOIN student_tuition_summary t ON p.student_id = t.student_id \"\n        \"WHERE p.student_id = ?;\";\n\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(read_model_db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK) {\n        sqlite3_bind_int64(stmt, 1, (sqlite3_int64)student_id);\n\n        if (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_ROW) {\n            status_out->opt_in_consent = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 0) != 0;\n            status_out->tuition_balance_due = sqlite3_column_int64(stmt, 1);\n            strncpy(status_out->currency,\n                    (const char*)sqlite3_column_text(stmt, 2),\n                    sizeof(status_out->currency) - 1);\n            found = true;\n        }\n        sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    }\n\n    if (!found) {\n        /* No consent record = no opt-in (FERPA compliant default) */\n        status_out->opt_in_consent = false;\n        status_out->tuition_balance_due = 0;\n    }\n\n    return true;  /* Query succeeded (even if no data found) */\n}\n```\n\n### 5.4 FERPA Compliance Safeguards\n\nPer the compliance guard implementation in `/app/project/docs/lessons/L03_Regulatory_Compliance_in_Code.md`:\n\n1. **Explicit Consent Only**: Default is `opt_in_consent = false`\n2. **Consent Versioning**: Each consent update increments version number\n3. **Audit Trail**: All consent changes are event-sourced\n4. **Immediate Revocation**: Consent check happens at execution time, not at enrollment time\n5. **Description Scrubbing**: Use `ledger_ferpa_scrub()` (line 321 of `ledger.h`) on any student-identifiable information in ledger descriptions\n\n---\n\n## 6. 2: Core Logic** (Week 3-4)\n- Extend `disburse_stipend_saga.h` with new callbacks\n- Implement `apply_stipend_to_tuition` use case in bursar_service\n- Wire command handlers\n\n**Phase 3: $5000.00\n\n    stipend_disbursement_request_t req = {\n        .student_id = STUDENT_ID,\n        .stipend_cents = 200000,  // $2000.00\n        .currency = \"USD\"\n    };\n\n    saga_error_t err;\n    bool result = disburse_stipend_run(&req, &test_callbacks, &err);\n\n    assert(result == true);\n    assert(err.code == SAGA_OK);\n    assert(get_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID) == 300000);  // $3000.00 remaining\n    assert(get_auto_payment_count(STUDENT_ID) == 1);\n}\n\n/* Test: Saga skips auto-payment when consent is not granted */\nvoid test_auto_payment_no_consent(void) {\n    setup_student_with_consent(STUDENT_ID, false);  // No consent\n    setup_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID, 500000);\n\n    stipend_disbursement_request_t req = { /* ... */ };\n\n    saga_error_t err;\n    bool result = disburse_stipend_run(&req, &test_callbacks, &err);\n\n    assert(result == true);  // Saga succeeds\n    assert(get_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID) == 500000);  // Unchanged\n    assert(get_auto_payment_count(STUDENT_ID) == 0);\n}\n\n/* Test: Compensation reverses auto-payment on later failure */\nvoid test_auto_payment_compensation(void) {\n    setup_student_with_consent(STUDENT_ID, true);\n    setup_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID, 500000);\n\n    test_callbacks.publish_domain_event = failing_publish;  // Inject failure\n\n    saga_error_t err;\n    bool result = disburse_stipend_run(&req, &test_callbacks, &err);\n\n    assert(result == false);\n    assert(err.code == SAGA_ERR_EVENT_BUS);\n    assert(get_tuition_balance(STUDENT_ID) == 500000);  // Restored\n    assert(get_reversal_count(STUDENT_ID) == 1);  // Compensation ran\n}\n```\n\n### 7.3 Monitoring and Observability\n\nAdd OpenTelemetry spans (per production hardening checklist in `/app/project/docs/architecture/04_saga_pattern.md`):\n\n```c\n/* Tracing for auto-payment step */\nvoid trace_auto_payment_step(\n    const char *step_name,\n    uint64_t    student_id,\n    int64_t     amount,\n    bool        success)\n{\n    char trace_msg[256];\n    snprintf(trace_msg, sizeof(trace_msg),\n             \"[SAGA:AutoPayment] step=%s student=%\" PRIu64\n             \" amount=%\" PRId64 \" result=%s\",\n             step_name, student_id, amount,\n             success ? \"OK\" : \"FAILED\");\n\n    otel_span_add_event(current_span(), trace_msg);\n}\n```\n\n### 7.4 Feature Flag Configuration\n\n```c\n/* Runtime feature flag check */\nbool is_auto_payment_enabled(void) {\n    const char *flag = getenv(\"EDUPAY_AUTO_PAYMENT_ENABLED\");\n    return flag && *flag == '1';\n}\n\n/* In saga execution */\nif (is_auto_payment_enabled()) {\n    // Execute Step 6: Auto-payment\n    apply_stipend_to_tuition_if_eligible(req, cb, err_out);\n} else {\n    // Skip auto-payment (feature disabled)\n    log_info(\"Auto-payment feature disabled, skipping step 6\");\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## # Architectural Proposal: Tuition Auto-Payment Feature

**Document Version:** 1.0
**Date:** 2026-02-02
**Author:** Senior Software Architect
**Status:** Draft for Review

---

## Executive Summary

This document presents a detailed architectural proposal for implementing the new **Tuition Auto-Payment** feature in the EduPay Ledger Academy platform. The feature automatically applies a student's newly disbursed financial aid stipend towards their outstanding tuition balance, contingent upon explicit opt-in consent from the student.

The proposed design:
- **Extends the existing `DisburseStipendSaga`** rather than creating a new saga
- Maintains strict adherence to **Clean Architecture**, **CQRS/Event Sourcing**, and the **Saga Pattern**
- Ensures **regulatory compliance** (FERPA, PCI-DSS) through consent-driven workflows
- Preserves **eventual consistency** across bounded contexts

## 1. Interaction Diagram/Sequence

### 1.1 High-Level Sequence Flow

The Tuition Auto-Payment feature introduces a new step in the stipend disbursement workflow that occurs **after** the stipend is successfully disbursed but **before** the saga completes. Below is the complete sequence:

```
┌─────────────────┐    ┌─────────────────────────┐    ┌─────────────────────────┐    ┌───────────────────┐    ┌───────────────────┐
│  Financial Aid  │    │ DisburseStipend
... (truncated)

      

      

        Bash Commands (10)
        
1. $ find /app/project -type f -name "*.md" | head -20
2. $ ls -la /app/project/
3. $ find /app/project/src -type d | head -30
4. $ tree /app/project/src -L 3 2>/dev/null || find /app/project/src -type d | sort | sed 's|[^/]*/|  |g'
5. $ find /app/project -name "*.c" -o -name "*.h" | wc -l
6. $ ls -la /app/project/src/core/
7. $ ls -la /app/project/src/services/
8. $ wc -l /app/project/src/core/cqrs/*.{h,c} 2>/dev/null | tail -1
9. $ find /app/project/docs -name "*.md" | sort
10. $ ls -lah /app/project/src/shared_kernel/
